                 《楞嚴經》修學
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 修學《楞嚴經》 淨界法師：《楞嚴經》講什麼？ 把心帶回家 海公在講《楞嚴經》講一個觀念說,所有的《楞嚴經》的經文沒有離開你的當下的身心世界,不管它再怎麼談玄說妙,都是在講你現在的身心世界。所以它是就著因緣來發明真理,沒有離開你的身心世界。所以這個十法界就是你的身心世界。那麼身心世界從內心來說,它是事造理具。事造就是講隨緣的作用,理具是講不變。那麼從外境上來說是橫辨豎歷,橫辨就是隨緣,講到差別相,豎歷就是不變,講無差別相,它是非並非別。 　　《楞嚴經》的真如理,我們看它經文的結構,它要你先發明內心的真如,你的心先調整好,你的心先找到不變隨緣,隨緣不變。然後你再找外境,哦原來外境,你的身心世界是不變隨緣,隨緣不變,一切的外境也是不變隨緣,隨緣不變,這第二個。第三個它告訴你,你內心的真如跟外境的真如是什麼樣的關系,你怎麼用你內心的真如來帶動外境的真如。所以《楞嚴經》講真如理講三件事,第一個講內心的真如,第二個講外境的真如,第三個講內心的真如跟外境的真如有什麼關系。這三個主題講了三卷半。

                </div>

                 Grieving is one of the most painful emotions we must endure in our lifetime. Here at Grieving-Messages From Heaven, we will help you in finding comfort and peace of mind by helping you in understanding the grieving process and help provide messages from your passed loved ones. Only one reading per family per picture. Reiki healing sessions for Grieving members will also be offered. So, join us and allow us to be of service to you. Update: Due to the high demand and need of hearing from passed loved ones, there is a six month waiting period. If you’re willing to wait six months, then you may post for a reading. We apologize for the wait. This is a nonprofit organization so they’re will be NO monetary gains. &gt;&gt;&gt; We will experience a backlog as we have many requests. Thank you in advance for your patience. &lt;&lt;&lt; By requesting membership of this group, you are agreeing to all terms and rules of this group.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Single Muslims Of California
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Mission Statement and Vision: This group was created to provide an online platform along with an in-person meetups/events to connect Single Muslims locally in a safe environment, where singles can make new friends and search for a spark with the intention of finding their future significant other. Disclaimer: This is not a matchmaking group, the intent of the Single Muslims of California group is to enhance the quality and understanding of relationships for Muslims while providing a safe environment for members to meet in person and connect online. SMOC does not tolerate or permit any political views, religious extremism, and violent acts that may cause harm to anyone directly or indirectly. The Admins and members are not responsible for any wrong actions taken by any individual that is currently part of the SMOC group. The Admins will do their best to help facilitate and maintain a safe environment. We ask that members are patient and considerate with one another and the efforts that each member (Admins included) puts forth. Rules: 1. Must be 18+. 2. Must provide an introduction of oneself. 3. No double dating as an act of respect to others. 4. Respect the privacy of the interaction of other members. 5. If things don't work out, move forward in a mature manner. Any violation to the rules may lead to a member’s removal from the group. Please bring up any concerns you may have towards anything/anyone violating the rules to one of the admins. Guidelines: The guidelines are not required, though, we encourage any member to use them as needed. 1. We encourage all members to have a profile photo of themselves. 2. Be active on the group by posting, commenting, and interacting with others 3. If you like someone, feel free to message them and get to know them better, then ask them out for a date. 4. It is preferred to message someone while/before adding them as a friend. 5. Encourage yourself to make friends with other members. 6. If you are shy and in need for an admin to help for a first time introduction to one of the members then feel free to ask as we are here to help you. 7. Check your inbox for any incoming message requests on a regular basis. 8. Keep your posts on the group's wall relevant to the group's purpose. 9. If you are unsure of what to say in your introduction, here are some information you may use as your guide: -A quick bio about your history. -Simple information on our career/educational paths. -Interests and hobbies. -Who you are as a person. -What your passions are. -What drives you in life.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Jewish Cooking
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Jewish Cooking with Joan Nathan! http://joannathan.com/ This group is for anyone interested in tips and recipes from Joan Nathan and/or just discussing Jewish cooking in general Jewish food is found in all corners of the world, encompassing various culinary styles. Following the same dietary laws and relying on local ingredients, Jews have developed their own regional flavors. This group is a place to discuss beloved classics and new favorites. When posting recipes, please ensure to comply with the Jewish dietary laws. While not everyone follows kosher rules, the laws remain a defining element in Jewish cooking. Specifically, please do not post recipes containing pork products, shellfish, or recipes containing dairy and meat together. Posts not fitting these parameters will be removed. Thank you for your interest in Jewish cooking!

               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 📖📚一乘真因淨土念佛法門
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  淨空法師: 🙏修淨土的人就是、修普賢菩薩十大願王、一乘大法! 已經給我們明顯的顯示出來，「咸共遵修普賢大士之德」，這就說明淨宗法門彌陀淨土是一乘大法，比大乘還要殊勝。 大乘是菩薩乘，小乘是聲聞乘，一乘是佛乘，一佛乘，在大乘之上。 隋唐時代是中國佛教的黃金時代，大小乘十個宗派都是那個時候建立的。 📽按此閱讀影片🎥https://youtu.be/4mzGcvomExM 🔴每個宗派的創始人，這祖師大德都是修行證果的人，不是普通人。 政治清明，眾生有福，佛菩薩統統都降臨了，應化在中國，給中國帶來了佛法盛世。 這些祖師大德們，幾乎是公認世尊四十九年所說的一切法，一乘只有三部經，是給你講一生成佛的，第一是《華嚴》，第二是《法華》，第三是《梵網》。 《梵網》沒傳到中國來，《華嚴》、《法華》傳來了，《梵網》只有一品，「菩薩心地戒品」，全經沒傳來，只有一品。 《法華》、《華嚴》到最後都是歸向淨土。 《華嚴》最明顯，你看到末後，善財五十三參，文殊普賢十大願王導歸極樂。 導歸極樂就歸《無量壽經》，《無量壽經》是什麼地位？ 一乘的一乘，這也是祖師大德們說的，《華嚴》、《法華》引導我們入彌陀淨土，引導我們往生西方極樂世界。 祖師大德這一句話，我是深有同感。 為什麼？我信淨土是從《華嚴》認識的，從《華嚴》、從《法華》、從《楞嚴》，這三部大經引導我歸向淨土，皈依淨宗法門，不容易！所以修淨土的人，就是修普賢菩薩十大願王。 西方極樂世界全是修普賢大行，這是古大德說的，「菩薩不修普賢行，不能圓成佛道」，他成不了佛。 所以大乘菩薩到最後，一定要接受普賢菩薩的教誨，才能夠圓滿成就。 而怎麼圓滿成就？原來都是普賢菩薩領導大家到極樂世界去成就的，你說這個多殊勝！佛法講無量的莊嚴，無比的莊嚴。 我們了解這一樁事，真正體會到這個境界，才一心皈依淨土，真的搞清楚，真的搞明白了。 （淨空老和尚開示） 念老在此地引《彌陀要解》，以「厭離娑婆，欣求極樂」為願。這幾個字重要，我們這一生有什麼願望？這就幾個字，厭離娑婆，欣求極樂，這就對了。「又以信願持名為，一乘真因」，一乘是上上乘法，比大乘還高。佛法裡頭講小乘，阿羅漢、辟支佛；大乘，菩薩；一乘是如來，諸佛如來。信願持名這四個字，一乘真因，我們要把它掌握到，不能疏忽。要像海賢老和尚一樣，真信切願，求生這個願非常懇切，佛號不中斷，持名就是念佛。有信有願，念這句佛號，這就是一乘真因。一乘真因是佛法的究竟圓滿，我們千萬不要輕易看過。 「故知世尊勸諭，正是往生切要」。釋迦牟尼佛勸導的，教誨我們，許多人不知道，正是往生的切要，這還得了！我們一生要的是什麼？念念要的就是這個。沒想到，世尊幾乎常常掛在嘴上，勸導我們，信、願、持名。勸我們「發此自覺覺他之大心」，真正相信是自覺，勸告別人是覺他，功德跟世尊沒有兩樣，勸念佛，不是勸別的。 「念佛名號，才契本經之宗」，宗是宗旨、宗趣，是這部經上講的最重要的一句話，就是「發菩提心，一向專念」。菩提是梵語，翻成中國的意思是覺悟。什麼人覺悟了？信願持名的人覺悟了，老實念佛的人覺悟了，把佛號忘掉的人是迷惑顛倒。我們今天怎麼辦？念念不能離開阿彌陀佛，其他的統統放下。為什麼？全是假的。這個話海賢老和尚常常勸人，好好念佛，其他的都是假的。 文摘恭錄自　淨土大經科註（第四回）第408集2016/12/28= 
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Indigo Adults
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Strangers in a Strange Land (The Adult Indigo) Is life on this earth painful for you? Do you ever feel as if you do not belong here? Do you ever feel as if you have been hiding your real Self all your life? Do you ever have to deny your real knowing in order to “get along”? Do you ever feel as if even those closest to you do not know the real you? Do you think of yourself as a failure? Do you feel as if you never experience real joy? Do you yearn for a place that feels like “home”? If these questions resonate within you and touch your heart and soul at their deepest place, you may be an Adult Indigo, still carrying, and suffering from the emotional wounds of childhood. For you, life on this Earth has probably been, and continues to be, confusing and difficult. Your inherent knowing is not acknowledged. Your intuitive wisdom is not honored. Your felt-sense of experience is not embraced. Almost no one understands or appreciate you. You try and try to “go along” and to “get along”, but, in your own eyes, almost everything you do fails. The only way you have been able to exist in this world is to deny the essence of your Being. Your Light has been dimmed, and your greatness has been diminished; you feel invisible. You feel that you are cut off from your Source and your Spirit. You feel alone and lonely. And you wonder why you feel sadness and depression. The Indigo children, who are born into Earth as pure Light channels of God, remember more and more eternal knowledge, secrets from the Other Side and hold the God-vision of a perfect world. These “old souls”, have come to embody a massive paradigm shift for our entire universe and to lead us toward ever-expanding world consciousness and a perfected world. Because of their inherent wisdom, knowing, and vision, they often have a hard time getting along in this world that does not understand or appreciate their uniqueness and their special gifts. This great dissonance between their perfect knowing and this Earth experience causes them tremendous pain and anguish. Their parents, teachers and society as a whole misunderstand this pain. Most try to help in more traditional and conventional ways, but fail. The attempts to heal on the rational, intellectual and cognitive level, do not work. The Indigo’s pain is the existential angst and loneliness that is caused by their separation and disconnection from God; by the dissonance they feel between their knowing of what a perfected world can be, and their experience of the world as it is. Their emotional pain resides on the spiritual, energetic, soul level, and that is where their pain must be healed. You, the Adult Indigo, at the deepest level, resonate with all the characteristics and the emotional pain of the Indigo Children. Today, more than 80% of the children being born are Indigos. The Indigos first started coming into this Earth at the rate of perhaps 5%-10% per year, right after WWII. You were one of these Indigos. And there were not many like you when you were young! During your childhood, you may have had a unique perspective on life that was probably not shared by members of your family, by classmates and friends or by teachers and coaches. You “got it” far more swiftly than anyone else, you may have felt “out of place” and wondered what you were doing here. You may have felt constantly “out of sync” with the rest of the world. You were a visitor in a foreign land, questioning the whys of things that made no sense to you. On a spiritual, energetic level, you felt the pain of the dissonance between your knowing and your everyday reality. But, your spiritual woundings were unrecognized and unhealed, and you have carried those spiritual woundings into adulthood. It is those unhealed spiritual woundings that are a cause of your angst and anguish; the cause of your discomfort with having to function in this world; the cause of your dissonance with being in body and being on Earth. As an early Indigo, you quickly learned that the world could not handle the full truth of who you are, the full expression of your Point of Essence. (POE) Your POE is the place where you are connected to God. Your POE is the place of your “I Am Presence”, your “GodSelf”. Your POE is the place where ego melts away, and where you are your unique ultimate Self. Your POE is the truth of who “You” are. As an early Indigo, you intuitively understood that if you were to survive and function in this world, you had to hide your true Essence. So, for most of your life, you have been disconnected from your “true Self”. 
                </div>

                 Great Hinduism
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is dedicated to Hinduism (Sanatan Dharma) &amp; only allowed for Hindus (Sanatani) &amp; those who have pure devotion &amp; strong belief in Hinduism (Sanatan Dharma) . We usually discuss about Hinduism related topics such as Hindu Festivals, Rituals, Dharma Vani, Bhagwan, Deities, persecution upon Hindus etc. in this group. But sometimes some unexpected activities are noticed here which disturb the purity &amp; environment of the group. So to prevent the group from such disturbances some rules have been made that members should follow : 1. Any kind of political activitiy, irreligious ad &amp; post are strictly prohibited here. 2. If a member misbehaves with other members without any logical reason, uses vulger language, makes fun of Bhagwan then he/she will be removed. 3. If you want to add people, then you can add only Hindus from any country. But if anybody add non-Hindus (Muslims, Christians, Buddhists, Sikhs, Jains, Jews, Pagans, Confuciasts, Taoists &amp; others), then the adder will be removed. 4. The intention of this group is to unite all Hindus over the world. Remember we all are Hindu. But if anybody tries to break our unity fighting on the basis of Castism &amp; Sects of Sanatan Dharma such as Brahmin, Shudra, Vaishnav, Shaivite then he/she will be removed. I hope all my Hindu brothers &amp; sisters will follow these rules &amp; will help us to make a strong Hindu brotherhood. Always follow Dharma, Dharma will protect you. _/\_ Namaste Jay Hinduism

NO POLITICS OR POLITICAL DISCUSSIONS will be allowed as a Post or in Comments. Any seen by the Administrator will be immediately deleted. NO POSTS ASKING FOR FINANCIAL HELP will be approved.                 </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 GROUP RULES WELCOME to the, "100% FREE Psychic Readings," group on Facebook. 100% FREE OF CHARGE All psychic readings performed by approved readers on the group page are 100% FREE OF CHARGE unconditionally, for pleasure, not profit. Advertising private paid readings publicly via direct posts, LIVE video broadcasts (Direct or shared), or Comments on the group page is strictly prohibited. Moderators are 100% FREE. Pre-Approved readers might read for a fee in private. Anybody who advertises paid services and/or charges on the group page, is out. PROTECTING THE VULNERABLE IS A KEY PRIORITY Protecting the vulnerable is a key priority. Posts that contain sensitive data like full date of birth details, pictures of children *Persons under the age of 18 years) and/or material considered inappropriate is strictly prohibited. COMMENTS ON MOST POSTS ARE TURNED OFF Comments on most posts are turned off in an attempt to prevent undesirable content such as abusive remarks and unsolicited advertising of private paid readings on the group page. Approved readers who are moderators however, can respond in the Comments section of a reading request post if they feel drawn. FINANCIAL, HEALTH, LEGAL &amp; PREGNANCY QUESTIONS Approved readers do not offer advice on financial, health, legal or pregnancy-related issues publicly on the group page. Requests for advice on financial, health, legal or pregnancy-related issues publicly on the group page are strictly prohibited. THE ADMIN TEAM DO NOT MODERATE PRIVATE MESSAGES The Admin Team only moderates public activity on the group page. They do not administrate the private lives of group members and are not responsible for the behaviour of group members in Private Messaging. HOW TO GET A READING WHEN YOU ARE READY People who say what they want help with, are ready to get the help they deserve. People who know who they want to contact on The Other Side are ready for a message. If you are not ready, that's OK. Just please don't post for attention only, as you will be ignored. HOW TO BECOME AN APPROVED READER If you are a reader and would like to share your gift 100% FREE OF CHARGE as an Approved Reader, unconditionally on the group page without competitions or arbitrary rules, please contact the group owner, Crow Edward Jenkins. If you post an offer to do readings before you have been approved, you and your pending post will be removed from the group. ……… Love &amp; Light, Crow Edward Jenkins (Owner/Admin.

           <div class="_8sz1 _8sz5 _8szd _8szj" id="u_0_1w">
            <div class="_8t03 _8tm_">
             <a class="_8ulx" href="/groups/628377447371412/">
              <div class="_8uly">
               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 夢參老和尚弘法資料平台
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  夢參老和尚略傳 一九一五年六月，夢參老和上出生於中國黑龍江省開通縣。 一九三一年，夢老在北京海淀藥王寺禮上修下林和上祝髮，法名「覺醒」，乃北五台「臨濟」派下「本覺昌隆 能仁聖果」法脈。因自覺大夢未醒，故自號「夢参」。同年，在北京拈花寺禮上量下源和上受比丘戒，戒期圓滿，南下九華山，朝禮地藏菩薩道場，正遇上六十年舉行一次開啟地藏菩薩肉身塔法會。由於因緣殊勝，為老和上爾後弘揚地藏法門伏下深遠的影響。 一九三二年，夢老轉赴福建省福州市鼓山湧泉寺參訪，對湧泉寺當時的一切境界覺似曾相識，彷彿重遊故地。當時虛雲老和上於鼓山創辦法界學苑，並請慈舟老法師主講《華嚴經》，夢老遂決定依止慈舟老法師學習《華嚴經》，歷時半年，仍無法契入華嚴義海，遂親自向慈舟老法師請法，之後決定以拜誦《普賢行願品》、燃身臂供佛，藉此苦行開啟智慧。 一九三五年，夢老在鼓山法界學苑學習《華嚴經》五年圓滿，當時的同學包括了臺灣的道源長老、靈源長老、慧三長老及大陸的淨嚴法師。 夢老除依止慈舟老法師學習《華嚴經》外，更旁及虛雲老和上的禪法，有時也奉慈舟老法師之指示，代講經論，諸如《阿彌陀經》等。 一九三六年，夢老赴青島湛山寺，依止倓虛老法師學天臺四教，並擔任湛山寺書記，負責倓虛老法師的庶務以及對外連絡事宜。在湛山寺擔任書記期間，夢老一方面向倓虛老法師學習天臺四教，及宣揚慈舟老法師的戒律精神。隨後奉倓虛老法師之命，禮請慈舟老法師北上青島湛山寺講律，又護送慈舟老法師到北京，開講《華嚴經》。 一九三六年底，夢老再度奉倓虛老法師之命，赴福建廈門萬石嚴，禮請弘一大師北上宏律，歷時半年之久。由於《梵網經》的講法因緣，弘一大師同意北上湛山寺，開講《隨機羯磨》。 一九三七年，擔任弘一大師的外護半年，深受弘一大師身教的啟發，當時並就近依《占察善惡業報經》所描述的占察輪相，請弘一大師親自製作一付，以供修習。弘一大師為了答謝他擔任半年的外護，親贈手書的《淨行品》偈頌乙本。 一九三七年至四○年，隨同倓虛老法師在長春般若寺傳戒，講四分戒律，並往來於東北各省、北京、天津、山東等地，講經弘法。其間曾接觸來自西藏的藏僧，引動了赴藏學習密法的因緣。 一九四○年，由北京至香港、新加坡、印度弘法並朝禮佛陀遺跡。 一九四一年，轉赴西藏拉薩學習密法，在西藏黃教三大寺之一的色拉寺學經論五年，依止第十世班禪師赤江仁波切，以靈倉仁波切，以及因能海法師引進參拜康薩仁波切。 一九四五年至一九四九年，轉赴西康等地參學，總計在西藏學習密法達十年之久。 一九五○年，中華人民共和國建立之初，由西藏返回中國內地，蒙受反共反革命之嫌而被判刑十五年，下放勞改十八年，總計入獄長達三十三年之久。在獄中，他經常觀想一句偈頌：「假使熱鐵輪，在汝頂上旋，終不以此苦，退失菩提心。」藉此度過重重磨難，奠立爾後重回教內弘揚佛法的信心。 一九八二年，受平反而出獄，回北京任教於北京中國佛學院。在這段期間，如法修學地藏法門，重啟弘揚經論的智慧。 一九八五年，接受福建南普陀寺妙湛老和上、圓拙長老之邀，到廈門南普陀寺重建閩南佛學院，並擔任教務長一職，開講《華嚴經》、《法華經》、《楞嚴經》、《大乘起信論》等。 一九八七年，應美國萬佛城宣化上人之邀，赴美數月後返回中國。 一九八九年，應美國洛杉磯妙法院旭朗法師之請，再次赴美弘法，開講《占察善惡業報經》、《華嚴經‧普賢行願品》、《地藏經》、《心經》、《金剛經》等，此後即旅居於美加地區。 一九九一年，於年中應台北居士之請，在新店開講《占察善惡業報經》，原本不收弟子的夢老，在該年底，由於種種因緣而收了生平第一位弟子，為其剃度，賜法號「繼夢」。夢參、繼夢師徒二人，只見二次面就定了此緣，實乃法界因緣及《華嚴經》不可思議之加持！其後，夢老陸續在寧波西街花園精舍開講《法界三觀》，及清泉會舘講《華嚴經‧淨行品》。 一九九五年，旅居加拿大溫哥華地區的三寶弟子，特別禮請夢參老和上講《十輪經》。 二○○○年，夢老於浙江重建雁蕩山祖庭。 二○○三至二○○七年，夢老駐錫山西五台山普壽寺講《華嚴經》。 夢參老和上出家後，雖遍參耆宿，顯密雙修，卻從未以一宗一派自居，畢生講筵不絕，但隨緣度眾，廣結法緣。據親近老和上的再傳弟子口述，援引夢老旅台弘法期間之生活趣事三則，以窺老人家隨機教化，妙趣橫生之方便智慧。 (一) 某日，老和上見侍者著一新拖鞋即道：「你哪來新鞋？」 侍者解釋：「信徒送的！你也有一雙啊！我有！你一定有！你有！我不一定有！」 老和上重拍腹部道：「我肚皮上被醫生挖了個洞，這個我有，你沒有，你要不要？」 在座者哄堂大笑，侍者亦不禁莞爾。 (二) 午後陽光斜照在電視螢幕上，侍者手持遙控器啪啪不斷地變換頻道，老和上見狀，請侍者把遙控器遞給他，只見老和上按著遙控器一會兒開一會兒關，速度之快令人目不暇給。 侍者莫名其妙，問道：「幹啥啊？」 老和上再重覆一次開關的動作：「幹啥？這叫生滅法！還看！」 (三) 講座完畢有信眾請求開示。 信眾問道：「老和上，我讀誦《金剛經》十多年一點都不懂，是不是該換一部經念？」 老和上云：「我讀誦《金剛經》六十多年也才懂一點點，現在還讀誦，那你念不念呢？」 (編案：本文關於夢參老和上之資料，皆取自其著作及自述。)
                </div>
               </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Light Of Rumi
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Jalaluddin Rumi was born in 1207 in Balkh in present-day Afghanistan. Increasing Mongol incursions when he was around the age of eleven forced his family to leave Afghanistan, who travelled to Baghdad, Mecca, Damascus and finally settled in Konya in Turkey. Rumi lived here for most of his life. Rumi was the son of a renowned Sufi scholar, and it is more than likely that he was introduced to Sufism from a young age. Sufism is a branch of Islam primarily concerned with developing the spirituality, or more precisely the inner character, of a Muslim. Both he and his father were firm believers in the revelations of the Qur'an, but criticised the mere outwardly legal and ritual practice that was being promoted at the time. In fact, much of his work is dedicated to waking people up, and encouraging them to experience life themselves, rather blindly following the scholars of the day. Rumi spent his early years, like many Muslims of the time, learning and studying Arabic, law, ahadith (the body of sayings of the Prophet Muhammad), history, the Qur'an, theology, philosophy, mathematics and astronomy. By the time of his father's death he had become an outstanding scholar in his own right, and took over his father's position as one of the highest scholars in the country at the young age of 24. He spent his time teaching and giving lectures to the public, and until the age of about 35, lived a fairly non-descript life. Then in 1244 Rumi met a travelling Sufi, called Shams (or Shamsi Tabrizi) and the whole course of his life changed. Shams became fast friends with Rumi, in whom he recognised a kindred spirit. The two developed a very close friendship and it was at this point that Rumi became more and more secluded, shunning the society of those he previously would discuss and debate matters with. His relationship with Shams caused great jealousy in his family and other students, and after a few years, Shams disappeared. Many believe he was murdered, but Rumi himself did not think so. He travelled for years looking for his friend, and it was this loss that led to the outpouring of his soul through his poetry. He wrote numerous lines of love poetry, called ghazals, but though they outwardly seem to be about Shams, it is not difficult to see that they are in fact poems describing his overpowering love of God. Shams' effect on Rumi was decisive. Whereas Rumi had before preached Islam soberly, he became, through Shams' influence, filled with the love of God. What was inside his soul finally came out. 
                </div>

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Evolution Science vs Creation Science
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is meant for science minded evolutionists and creationists to debate and defend their beliefs using science. Both creationists and evolutionists claim scientific evidence supports their beliefs. This group will allow them the opportunity to prove that position through the evidence. Rules: * Any science related topic may be discussed including biology, genetics, astronomy, geology, paleontology and physics. * Be respectful * No blocking other members * No ganging up on others. If you are asked to leave a debate by the person who made the post or an admin, you must comply. You can start up a new post. * Only scientific data will be accepted when challenging someone's beliefs. No one will take you word for it. If someone asks you for cited references, you must comply or accept defeat. * No YouTube videos, memes and bible verses in original posts. However, a video or meme may be used to help clarify scientific research already posted. * Bible verses and references to the metaphysical world are not accepted. I understand they are the staple of the creationist faith, however this debate group is meant for science minded Christians to defend their beliefs using scientific evidence. In order for two people to debate effectively, they both must be on the same page of reality. * You may not use God, the devil or any other metaphysical being to disprove scientific research and evidence. * If you request evidence and someone takes the time to present that evidence, have the courtesy to read through their research, so you may intelligently discuss and debate the subject. Two people standing on their soap boxes yelling at each other is unproductive and frustrating. * All original posts must include a written explanation for links to research. Any posts including only a hyperlink will be removed. * All original posts should have a link to a science related article/paper along with a written description in your own words explaining the articles content and what you'd like to discuss. A clear description in your own words stating an explanation of the subject matter and the topic of discussion can replace a link to an article. * No memes in original posts * Memes can be used in a post's feed as long as they are not insulting, not vulgar and are not used in great excess to spam/troll the feed * This is a debate group for science minded adults, and I expect everyone to act in that manner. If you make a claim and someone asks you to provide them evidence, you must do so or abandon the discussion. "Im right because I say so" will not be accepted. * Have fun and learn from each other.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 念佛-阿彌陀佛
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 →尊敬的師兄師姐們請在此了解小組版規← 各位慈悲的師兄師姐們，大家好 歡迎加入「念佛-阿彌陀佛」小組，該小組主要發 「淨空法師」 的白話文章，所以只有信任管理員在此面發帖，此小組不開放公共發帖，懇請見諒，同時也請大家不要在留言區發帖，如果大家想要在留言區發圖，小組只限制發佛菩薩或淨空法師的圖片，這是為了避免圖片太雜，謝謝合作。 歡迎大家也邀請您們的家人朋友加入此小組學習和分享佛法。 若小組有帶來大家的不便，懇請大家原諒。 阿彌陀佛 _/\_ 歡迎大家也關注 「阿彌陀佛」 專頁： https://www.facebook.com/amituofobuddha &lt; 以下信息只是給管理員 &gt; 【管理員發帖條規事項】 1.小組主要發 「淨空法師」 文章/視頻，若是其他法師或老師，目前允許的有：定弘法師，劉素雲老師。若有其他法師或老師的文章推薦，請先聯繫末學，需要經過同意才能發。小組發帖以教學為主，若是其他關於法師/老師生活報告情況，不建議頻密發，除非是一些特別情況。 2.管理員們發文章或視頻，需要在小組直接發，若是分享視頻，視頻要在10分鐘左右，若是分享文章，文章長短中等就好，不要太長。 3.發文章要帶法師/老師名字和文章標題，例如: 淨空法師：極樂世界，眾生生者，永無退轉 4.發文章要帶圖，圖只限制於： I.西方三聖，或西方三聖其中之一的佛菩薩，II.釋迦摩尼佛，III.淨空法師，IV.簡單的圖文標題 （如果是其他菩薩，除非是和貼文的標題有關系也可以） 例如如下： 佛菩薩圖 https://goo.gl/z36r5H 淨空法師圖 https://goo.gl/hxI9I2 簡單的圖文標題 https://goo.gl/89tk7i 圖裡帶文章 例如：https://goo.gl/aX6iFt 特別注意：選擇佛菩薩圖要選傳統式的，若關於圖方面有哪裡不明白，請與末學聯繫。 5.一個帖裡面只能發一篇文章和一張圖，不能一篇文章幾張圖或幾篇文章一張圖。（因情況而定，除非圖片有關聯） 6.每位管理員一星期最少要有2-3次發文章，每次發帖一天不超過三篇文章，這是為了保護文章不會沈底太快，影響瀏覽量不集。 7.若有管理員因一些原因無法繼續一星期最少2-3次發帖，請及時告知末學。若是太久沒發帖，末學可能會安排讓位給其他有緣人。（末學會根據不同情況做決定） 8.小組一切的管理由創始人(原主)管理，新加入的成員請不要自行通過，也不要取消和置頂帖子，一切由小組創始人(原主)管理，管理員們只負責發帖，若發現有毀謗，惡搞，廣告等等不良留言，管理員們可以幫忙刪除留言，若有不確定性，可以及時聯繫末學。 在此也感謝所有管理員們為社團的無私付出。 阿彌陀佛 _/\_ 願此小組功德，莊嚴佛淨土， 上報四重恩，下濟三途苦， 若有見聞者，悉發菩提心， 盡此一報身，同生極樂國。 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 WARRIORS OF LIGHT AND LIGHT KEEPERS
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 welcome to this special place where love is for all. this group is for all that defend what is right and just, and for those that feel sometimes in need of a shelter... so that they can keep on being warriors of peace &amp; beings of light. we work for peace and defend the good and the true. may you be in peace always. **************************************** see also: MEDITATIONS , PRAYERS for PEACE and LOVE http://www.facebook.com/group.php?v=info&amp;ref=ts&amp;gid=181488436646 **************************************** The term ‘Warrior’ seems to conjure up visions of battle and bloodshed in most people and yet the only thing that a Warrior of Light wishes to shed is their own Darkness, so that they may better assist others in increasing their own Light. The Master Teachers once described the Spiritual Warrior in this way: “Each and every one of you, is a being of Light. But there are those who have agreed to come forth in this time and defend the honor of the Light, those who are Spiritual Warriors. It is difficult for many to accept that of the position of a Spiritual Warrior. They need to realize that which is to be accomplished. The more that they struggle against it, the more that they become dark and the more that they struggle against it. It then becomes an endless battle within themselves, their life and their environment.” And so with this explanation I want to ask you to discover for yourself, in your own way, what does it mean to “defend the honor of the Light”? And what of this “battle”? All of us have both Darkness and Light within us. So it is a battle that is most often fought within ourselves to emphasize and increase the Light, within ourselves and others. This is the battle that the Spiritual Warrior is involved in. It is a battle to always be Light or positive, to never promote Darkness or negativity and to never allow Darkness or negativity to continue unchallenged. As a Warrior of Light we must first Give, to Live. But what is it that we must give? The answer to this question lies within each of us. Each of us is a unique solution to a specific situation which God has sent us here to correct. This means that you alone have a special Light to use in your mission here which no one else can use in the same way as you can. What is your mission? What is your Light? Why are you here? Search deep within yourself, for when you Give of your Light which God has sent you here to share for the All, you will truly Live a life you can only dream of. God has many gifts in store for you, isn't it time that you received them? by Shoshana Byrne

                 Atheists
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Mission Statement: Our mission is to create and encourage a global community of Atheists and to find common ground where we are able; in order to work together towards a world of reason and logic. RULES UPDATED: July 11th, 2017 Summary of Bannable Offenses 1. Personally attacking other members of our group. (Name calling, ad hominems, malicious reporting, defamatory statements, etc...) 2. Offensive content: Nudity, sexist comments, rape jokes, disparaging of disabilities, racism, anti-Semitic, misgendering, or attempts to violate the spirit of this rule. 3. Blocking Admin Team. The Admin/Mod names are available in the member list. 4.Posting non-public content of our members without blocking out their names in a post in this group or in other locations. 5. Repeat minor offenses. (Note: The Admin team may give you a warning first or remove you from the group without notification, based on the offense.) Admin promise to you: We will evaluate every suspected rule violation without ideological bias and make decisions as an Admin team prior to removing or banning any member of the group. If you feel you were unjustly banned, you may request a review by the Admins. POSTS: Please moderate your own posts for these rule infractions. See REPORTING if there are any rule violations that you can't handle. SUBJECT MATTER: Anything that doesn't violate a rule of Facebook or one of the group rules is appropriate. We are a group of Atheists, this is not necessarily a group about Atheism. SPAM: Please don't spam the same subject matter in the group, on the same day. Don’t start a new thread referring to an old thread. Try to limit yourself to 3 OPs a day. IMAGES: All content posted to the group should be SFW (safe for work) If an image is NSFW (not safe for work), a member should post an external link with no preview with a tag NSFW. If you are unsure about an image, ask an Admin/Mod. TROLLING: Please do not intentionally troll the group. If you have something you want to discuss that will aggravate other members, please make an argument in your OP explaining your position. DISCUSSIONS: Should be related to the subject of the original post. Please do not “hi-jack” threads. If you feel antagonized by the other person, it may help to take a break or find common ground on the subject. We are here to be part of a community. REPORTING: Please tag or PM an Admin/Mod for issues with comments on a thread. You can also report a post to the Admin team instead of to Facebook and all of the Admins will see the post. THEIST ACCUSATIONS: Please do not accuse fellow members of being a theist. See REPORTING if you believe someone is not an atheist. FACEBOOK COMMUNITY STANDARDS: https://www.facebook.com/communitystandards

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Bhagavad Gita As It Is
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 DEAR READERS, Kindly join to learn more about Krishna Consciousness and daily be enlightened by one verse from the Bhagavad-Gita As It Is (with QA)(1972 Edition) and Srimad Bhagavatam by ISKCON Founder Acharya - His Divine Grace A.C. Bhaktivedanta Swami Prabhupada. This is a group for reading and discussion of verses from the Bhagavad-Gita As It Is and Srimad Bhagavatam by Srila Prabhupada. http://asitis.com/ http://prabhupadabooks.com/kb http://www.krishnapath.org/free-ebooks-audiobooks-of-srila-prabhupada/ http://gloriousgita.com/ Lord Sri Krishna is the Supreme Personality of Godhead. He is the original, primeval and Supreme Person who is simultaneously expanded everywhere throughout existence and yet is still situated in His eternal abode in His original, transcendental form. He is the all-powerful, all-knowing, and all-merciful Being. He is the chief eternal living entity amongst all eternal living entities who are His parts. He is responsible for fulfilling all the desires of the subordinate living entities since time immemorial. "I am the source of all spiritual and material worlds. Everything emanates from Me. The wise who perfectly know this engage in My devotional service and worship Me with all their hearts." - Bhagavad Gita 10.8 The Bhagavad-gita is universally renowned as the jewel of India's spiritual wisdom. Spoken by Lord Krishna, the Supreme Personality of Godhead to His intimate disciple Arjuna, the Gita's seven hundred concise verses provide a definitive guide to the science of self-realization. No other philosophical or religious work reveals, in such a lucid and profound way, the nature of consciousness, the self, the universe and the Supreme Personality of Godhead, Sri Krishna.

                 Study of Judaism
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 "Study of Judaism" is a group for the study of Tanakh, Mishneh Torah, Talmud, Shulchan Aruch and other authentic Jewish Scripture. Anyone who believes that HaShem is our G-d, HaShem is One, and HaShem's Torah is FOREVER without any other new, standard or revised versions is welcome to join our group. Please treat others as you would have them treat you. Attacks on fellow members and bigoted comments against other religion or against any other group of people will not be tolerated in this group and will result in immediate expulsion from the group. Requests for people to pray differently or requests for people to pray to deities other than the Jewish version of Hashem will result in expulsion from the group. This is not a forum discussion for comparative religion. Please don't start conversation threads with how other religions are different from Judaism or how the practice of Judaism is different from other religions. We believe in the truth of all of our Jewish writings and oral traditions and oral laws. Please refrain from any discussion which may question the validity or truth of any of our Jewish practice or faith. Please do not post any items for sale here regardless of their religious nature. Please do not post anything not specifically dealing with the study of Judaism. While we realize that there are many important topics regarding Israel and charity and politics relating to Jews - this is not the place.

                 Welcome to Witchcraft For Beginners. This is a place to share and learn about the craft, and people of all skill levels are welcome here. Feel free to post spells, curses, discussions, meditations, or anything that can be useful in the craft. **WE HAVE ADDED A LEGAL DISCLAIMER. READ IT IN UNDER "ANNOUNCEMENTS" ** (Comment "Read and Agreed" on that post). ** (Read all "ANNOUNCEMENTS" for last minute rule updates as well) ** RULES ARE AS FOLLOWS: **NO MENTION, OF WEED, CANNABIS, and its paraphernalia etc** (IT'S NOT LEGAL EVERYWHERE AND IT'S MENTION HAS NO PLACE IN THIS GROUP). Any comment or post mentioning it, will be REMOVED and so will the member responsible. ** NO FREE READINGS ARE TO BE OFFERED AT ANY TIME ** **(If you have paid reading services to offer, see number 5 below).** ** NO SHARING OF OTHER GROUPS HERE. USE YOUR PERSONAL PAGE FOR THAT. ** **YOU MUST GET a member's PERMISSION before "PMing", "INBOXING", or "ADDING" them. (Ask in the comments section of posts)** If you get PMs by someone in this group that does not have your permission, tell ADMIN. If you allow yourself to get scammed through PMs, WITCHCRAFT FOR BEGINNERS is not liable. **NO SELFIES** (Be mindful, this is NOT A DATING GROUP. Members will be removed if attempting to use it as such)** **SALES POSTS ON SUNDAYS ONLY** **EGG CLEANSING POSTS ON SUNDAYS ONLY** **NO POLITICS** **NO MENTION OF V-I-R-U-S AND/OR RELATED** (Members will BE REMOVED if doing so). 1. BE NICE. No personal attacks, or rude behavior will be tolerated. It's ok to disagree with someone, but please keep it civil. 2. NO TROLLING. If you post about stuff that attracts negative reactions several times in a row, or something that will obviously upset people, the admin may consider it trolling. If a member is trolling please don't feed into it, let admin know. 3. NO BASHING OTHERS BELIEFS. No rude or disrespectful comments towards other member's belief systems, or practices. Like I said above, it's okay to disagree, but it's not okay to be rude about it. 4.NO PREACHING DOGMATIC BELIEFS. Comments about a "three fold law", the "ten fold law", statements such as, "If you do this and that, then demons will haunt you", or, "You'll have bad Karma". etc." are not allowed. (Such beliefs were invented to control people with fear). 5. SALES, PROMOTING MERCHANDISE. We allow sales promoting ONE day each week. That day is SUNDAY. ONE post. **(You must be a member of WITCHCRAFT FOR BEGINNERS to promote sales)**. 6. DO NOT BLOCK ADMIN, and/or MODERATORS. We can still see what you post, but cannot message you, thus moderate if needed. 7. DO NOT DISABLE MESSAGING for the same reason. Violation of these rules will result in a WARNING and repeat offenders will be REMOVED from the Witchcraft For Beginners group. If you have any questions, or concerns, feel free to PM an admin, and we will get it sorted out. *ADMINS* Avadar NightRaven (myself) Jade Snow.

                 Jewish Humor
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 "With so many negative events taking place around the planet, sometimes it is refreshing to stand back for a moment and enjoy a good laugh! The Bible says : "A merry heart doeth good like a medicine, but a broken spirit drieth the bones.." In our present troubled world, watching &amp; listening to some Jewish humor is just what the Jewish doctor ordered! We can't just sit there in misery &amp; negativity. Even in the concentration camps, Jews were humorous. Research has revealed that the Jews in concentration camps created plays, told jokes because the only thing they could do was laugh at their own predicament, sad as it was, because there was no other escape &amp; the only other alternative was to go crazy altogether! Feeling different, feeling alienated, feeling persecuted, feeling that the only way you can deal with the world is to laugh because if you don't laugh you're going to cry and never stop crying -- that's probably what's responsible for the Jews having developed such a great sense of humor. The people who had the greatest reason to weep, learned more than anyone else how to laugh. I welcome you &amp; all Jews with open arms! I'll do my best to keep everyone well entertained. Let this group be like sunshine and be a joy &amp; a blessing in everyone's life! "

In the future, we would be planning for 1 or 2 days trip too. 5) We also share our vast experience with temples that we carry with us. Now all the above-said things cannot be done without the support of our lovely members and all that we expect from you and the need of the hour is. 1) Do invite your friends and relatives to the group more the people more the reach to help a temple. 2) Strictly we avoid politics in the group as it always leads to arguments. 3) When you post information especially pics or videos please provide at least basic information about the temple. Random pics will look more like spam. 4) Please provide inputs to us where we can improve to help the community better. We are not Mr.Perfect to be right always. Stay Blessed and Enjoy your Stay.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 BILLY GRAHAM
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WELCOME to the Billy Graham Facebook Group! Now please click on "Invite People to Join," and invite all of your friends. Lets make this group the largest on Facebook to honor Dr. Graham. This is a group developed to support and honor one of the greatest known evangelist in our lifetime. He dedicated over 50 years of his life to the ministry and remains to be one of the most loved preacher and respected evangelist of all times. Please feel free to post pictures, comment on the wall, begin a discussion and invite others to join this group. PLEASE DO NOT post anything if it does not relate to Billy Graham or the Billy Graham Evangelistic Association, all other posts will be removed by the administrators of the group. __________________________________________ A LITTLE KNOWN FACT You may say "others are more significant and I will never get a chance, but one never know when God will call us to greatness." READ ON. . . Angel Martinez By Ted Elmore Should anyone question the success of Texas Baptists' mission efforts, look no further than the 10 most influential Texas Baptists of the 20th century. In that list is Angel Martinez, who in his personal testimony referred to himself as a "little shoe shine boy from San Antonio." Martinez was converted in a Baptist mission in San Antonio in July 1935 at the age of 13 and preached his first sermon in September of the same year. At the conclusion of that message, every member of his family except his father was converted to Christ. There was little if any doubt that God had called and ANGEL MARTINEZ Gifted Angel Martinez as an evangelist. He saw the wisdom of preparing to be an evangelist by receiving a solid education. He graduated from Baylor University in 1945 and Southern Baptist Theological Seminary in 1949. He conducted 51 revival meetings as a seminary student. His reputation spread beyond the seminary campus in Louisville, Ky. In those years, a committee from Los Angeles contacted him about a citywide crusade. Martinez politely thanked them, but refused, saying God had called him as a local-church evangelist, not as a crusade evangelist. The committee then went to their second choice, Billy Graham. The rest is history. It is a mark of greatness and security in the Lord when one can say to a great opportunity, "That is not what God has called me to do." One of Martinez's trademarks was his colorful dress. Walter K. Ayres told the story of his own call to ministry in an Angel Martinez revival meeting. Ayers, a former University of Arkansas football player, walked forward in blue jeans and T-shirt and said, "Dr. Martinez, God has called me to be an evangelist too!" According to Ayers, Martinez replied, "Always look sharp, young man. Always look sharp!" Martinez offered insightful advice to a young evangelist about 15 years ago: "Prepare one new sermon each week, whether you preach it or not. The evangelist must stay homiletically fresh." He always ended his message by giving the same invitation, almost word for word. "No matter what I preach, I always tell people how to be saved." He always shared the gospel. Martinez's ministry spanned 60 years. At age 73, God called him home to heaven. When he led inquirers in the "sinner's prayer," he would say, "If you prayed that little prayer with me, I will see you in heaven." Conservative estimates are that Martinez will see more than 500,000 who prayed that little prayer with him somewhere in a revival meeting mostly in a Southern Baptist church, many in Texas. We are admonished in Scripture to not despise the day of small beginnings. Would any in that little mission in San Antonio in 1935 have dreamed how God would use a 13-year-old Hispanic teenager? No wonder Texas Baptists said Angel Martinez was among their Top 10! Ted Elmore is associate director of evangelism for the Baptist General Convention of Texas 
                </div>
               </div>

This project lifts the Google worth of every single atheist website in the world. In doing so it helps advance our ideas further when compared against the outdated ideas of our counterparts. Rationalism and science must prevail, together we can play a role in that. If you have been invited to this group by a friend, it is because we assume you would want to be part of a project of this magnitude and importance.                  Atheist, Agnostic, and Non-Religious
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Positive support and discussion for atheists, agnostics, humanists, freethinkers, the Brights, secularists, and anyone who feels the pull of reason in need of a supportive group. Christians and other religious are welcome. However, this is a non-religious group, please keep that in mind when engaging with other members. (For those with thick skulls, recurrent proselytizing can earn a permanent ban.) -=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=- "More and more, as I think about history,' he pondered, 'I am convinced that everything that is worth while in the world had been accomplished by the free inquiring critical spirit and that the preservation of this spirit is more important than any social system whatsoever. But the men of ritual and the men of barbarism are capable of shutting up the men of science and of silencing them forever." --Sinclair Lewis "Our belief is not a belief. Our principles are not a faith. We do not rely solely upon science and reason, because these are necessary rather than sufficient factors, but we distrust anything that contradicts science or outrages reason." --Christopher Hitchens "A man's ethical behavior should be based effectually on sympathy, education, and social ties; no religious basis is necessary. Man would indeed be in a poor way if he had to be restrained by fear of punishment and hope of reward after death." --Albert Einstein "When I became convinced that the universe is natural, that all the ghosts and gods are myths, there entered into my brain, into my soul, into every drop of my blood the sense, the feeling, the joy of freedom. The walls of my prison crumbled and fell. The dungeon was flooded with light and all the bolts and bars and manacles became dust. I was no longer a servant, a serf, or a slave. There was for me no master in all the wide world, not even in infinite space. I was free--free to think, to express my thoughts--free to live my own ideal, free to live for myself and those I loved, free to use all my faculties, all my senses, free to spread imagination's wings, free to investigate, to guess and dream and hope, free to judge and determine for myself . . . I was free! I stood erect and fearlessly, joyously faced all worlds." --Robert G. Ingersoll "Although the time of death is approaching me, I am not afraid of dying and going to Hell or (what would be considerably worse) going to the popularized version of Heaven. I expect death to be nothingness and, for removing me from all possible fears of death, I am thankful to atheism." --Isaac Asimov, "On Religiosity," Free Inquiry †† "You do not need the bible to justify love, but no better tool has been invented to justify hate." --Richard A. Weatherwax "Why should I allow that same God to tell me how to raise my kids, who had to drown His own?" --Bertrand Russell ********************************** Quotes From The Faithful: "but i choose to believe in christ being my savior because i have to...i think that qualifies for thinking outside the box" --Christian flamer, Carlos Rodriguez, 09/15/2006 "How can atheists sue God?                  『彌勒家園公告聲明』本社團為非營利一貫道社團，秉持不分組別的精神，為推廣 彌勒祖師『無緣大慈，同體大悲』的精神，替師尊老大人 - 濟公活佛分擔三曹普的重責，因而在此為全球各組的道親提供一個網路平台，讓全球道親能學習更多真理，同時也藉以鼓勵各組在世界各國開荒辦道遇挫折的壇主人才們。高齡一百多歲的 基礎天基組 - 領導前人老 - 張粉前人老 慈悲︰「大家都是一師之徒、一母之子，應該不分你我，一同為三曹普渡盡心力」。 敬告社團會員們：本社團擁有審察權 和 不張貼權，若同一人在同一天張貼超過五則文章，本社團管理員有權決定張貼或刪減超過數量的文章以保障閱讀者與其他張貼文章的大德們的權力，敬請諒解，感恩慈悲。 若有任何道親在本社團所張貼分享來自 youtube 的仙佛聖歌影片，如有侵犯到貴單位 或 貴公司的版權 或 版權擁有者的版權， 後學在此 懇求貴公司 和 版權擁有者 您的慈悲寬恕，因為大家都是在不知有版權限制的情況下分享張貼 youtube 的聖歌網址，初發心都是為了宣傳 天恩師德，絕非惡意盜用！若真不能分享引用，後學在此懇請版權擁有的貴公司 與 版權擁有的前賢大德慈悲通知一下，本社團將會盡速刪除，後學也在此替違規的道親向版權擁有的公司與個人道歉， 同時也感謝版權擁有的公司 與 前賢大德們的慈悲。 (2020年4月2日 增加編寫此公告) 管理員︰後學 Kevin Chou 敬啟. ================================ 『 歡 迎 蒞 臨 彌 勒 家 園 』 彌勒佛是未來佛, 是當來下生彌勒尊佛, 2500年前, 如來世尊慈悲及交代, 如來涅槃後後500歲, 即是當今白陽時期, 彌勒當應運下生, 開設龍華三會廣度眾生. 第一會演說四聖諦 度92億, 斷煩惱結, 證阿羅漢果. 第二會, 演說十二因緣, 度94億, 度無明海, 證辟支佛果. 第三會, 演說六度波羅蜜, 度96億, 令眾發無上菩提心, 令眾生證菩薩果. 開設彌勒家園, 希大眾發心往生彌勒淨土, 和 彌勒愿力, 不殺生不吃肉, 修五戒十善, 拜佛念佛, 繫念彌勒稱彌勒名, 造立彌勒法相, 1. 犯罪懺悔, 下品往生. 2. 恭敬禮拜, 中品往生. 3. 修行六度, 上品往生. 求生彌勒內院煉就不退轉道心, 再隨彌勒下閻浮提廣度眾生證阿羅漢以上之果位, 最終究竟成佛. 南無當來下生彌勒尊佛.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Atheist Meme Repository
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello, and welcome to Atheist Meme Repository. This group is here so that we may find and share atheist memes of all kinds; from the very funny, to those that are more to the point &amp;/or serious. Memes are one of the most effective ways to share thoughts and make people aware of things. Thus, it is important to have groups and sites where people can help better educate and inform others of important facts &amp; information. Rules: We operate mainly on the honor system here. Admin relies upon members to report items to the Admin. No reporting to Facebook. Facebook already removes enough of our material as it is. Anyone caught reporting to FB instead of group Admin will be removed from the group. Update: Sometimes there are subjects presented which not everyone agrees with. However, a word of caution, there should be no name-calling of either other members or of the Admin. No personal insults, or any other form of attack upon individuals here. Doing so, will get you tossed out. We can agree to disagree and do so without resorting to the same things that we see in the patently religious. I guess that I have to add that there will be no advertising or promotion of ignorance, superstition, or religion of any kind. Please be aware that 'MeToo' is considered another belief-based religion here. And that is simply because they promote belief, over actual evidence. With that in mind, enjoy! And, please remember to share the great memes when you can. Cheers!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Pantheism
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is the most active Pantheism discussion board on the internet. "Pantheism essentially involves two assertions: that everything that exists constitutes a unity and that this all-inclusive unity is divine." (Alasdair MacIntyre, Ency of Philosophy, "Pantheism" 1971). This prominent definition is reiterated by philosopher Michael Levine who defines pantheism as the perception of "Divine Unity". http://www.pantheism.com for more **** Einstein, Spinoza, and other brilliant scientists, philosophers, artists, and thinkers speak of a God that is EVERYTHING, altogether. Is it time to reclaim the word God? All around the world, children are taught that God is limited; that God is a man; that God is not in control of "evil"; that God is angry and superficial. But some of us perceive that everything is God; everything is Divine. Thank you for joining us and "Like" the Pantheism fan page as well: http://www.facebook.com/pantheism.community **** By being in this group you agree to the following: * Public assaults are not tolerated. Avoid derogatory name calling and profanity. * Do not purposefully create conflict to gain attention (do not be a troll). * NO proselytizing: includes disrespectful promotion of (or preoccupation with) traditional theistic views in a pantheism forum, referring to God as "He", "Him" etc. Please keep in mind this group is about pantheism, where "God" (or "god") in this context means everything and does not mean a Christian, Muslim or any kind of theistic god. In speaking of those versions of god, please keep in mind where you are and please qualify your statements by stating that you are discussing the "personal god" or "Judeo-Christian God" etc. * NO political proselytizing: DO NOT ASSUME that all share your political concerns (veganism, your brand of environmentalism, libertarianism, etc.) Please relate your political opinions and concerns with discussions about pantheism. * Please stay relevant to topics. * Please assume good faith in others. We ALL slip up on occasion (i.e. get our feathers ruffled, etc.) and we all realize this happens. Avoid using Facebook's "blocking" feature in the group. * Please avoid removing your posts that have responses from others in consideration of those responses. * Please relate your post to the subject of pantheism. * Please do not advertise or post off topic items here. Posts that are judged off-topic, spam, click-bait, or promotional will be removed. USE, "REPORT TO ADMIN" ON THE TOP RIGHT OF EACH POST FOR VIOLATIONS. A warning, public or private, may be made prior to a permanent ban. If you do not respect these guidelines, you may leave the group at any time. This page is administered by volunteers (theparadiseproject.org) and is run as an independent freethinking forum for all. **** To turn off all email notifications: Account Settings&gt;Notifications&gt;Emails. Also, you can click on any group message on your Newsfeed and turn off Newsfeed updates as well.

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 LORD VENKATESHWARA (TIRUPATI BALAJI)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Tirumala Venkateswara Temple (Telugu: తిరుమల వేంకటేశ్వర దేవాలయం, Kannada: ತಿರುಮಲೆ ವೆಂಕಟೇಶ್ವರ ದೇವಾಲಯ, Tamil: திருமலை வேங்கடாசலபதி திருகோவில்), also known as Tirupati Venkateswara Temple is a famous Hindu Temple of Lord Venkateswara located in the hill town Tirumala, Andhra Pradesh. The temple is located on the Venkatachalam hill that forms part of the seven hills of Tirumala, and hence the temple is also known as the Temple of Seven Hills (Saptagiri in Sanskrit, Edukondalu in Telugu and Ezhumalai in Tamil). The presiding deity of the temple, Lord Venkateswara, is also known by other names - Balaji or Srinivasa or Perumal. The temple is the richest and the most visited place of worship in the world.The temple is visited by about 50,000 to 100,000 pilgrims daily, while on special occasions and festivals, like the annual Brahmotsavam, the number of pilgrims shoots up to 500,000, making it one of the most visited holy place in the world. The temple has a self-manifested idol murti of Lord Vishnu, with the Lord believed to have resided here for the entire Kali Yuga. In Sri Vaishnava tradition, the temple is considered one of the 108 Divya Desam sites.
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">20&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">278 篇新帖</span></span>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Jewish Spirit
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Jewish Spirit is a group for sharing ideas about the spiritual, philosophical, and intellectual sides of Judaism: ethnographic, historic, symbolic, Biblical, Talmudic, psychological, literary, and other deeper interpretations. Jewish Spirit looks beneath surface meanings in Jewish theology, values, and culture. Jewish Spirit promotes Jewish learning, prayer, forgiveness, deeds of loving kindness, consolation, healing, renewal, redemption, and finding God. Jewish Spirit respects and values all branches of Judaism; it is not limited to any one of them. Our main denomination is Judaism, in its spiritual entirety, fullness, and richness. Jewish Spirit presents an egalitarian viewpoint. It emphasizes the role of women, as in such fellow Facebook groups as Women of the Wall (WOW), Jewish Orthodox Feminist Alliance (JOFA), Women of Reform Judaism, and Hagbah: Where observant progressive feminists lift up Torah. Jewish Spirit welcomes previously under-represented groups, such as the LGBTQ community. It welcomes all ages and abilities. Members come from Ashkenazi, Sephardi, Nigerian, Ugandan, Lemba, Mizrahi, Mistaravi (Jews from Arab lands), Ethiopian, Indian, Persian, Indonesian, and other backgrounds, in approximately this order. Jewish Spirit seeks out far-flung Jewish communities. In addition to Western countries, members come from Nigeria, Uganda, Kenya, Brazil, Russia, South Africa, Poland, India, Ethiopia, the Philippines, Hungary, Ghana, Holland, China, New Zealand, Cambodia, Romania, Argentina, Turkey, Egypt, Indonesia, Thailand, Pakistan, Bangladesh, Cameroon, Portugal, Saudi Arabia, the United Arab Emirates, Vietnam, and elsewhere, in this order. Jewish Spirit reaches out to Jews of color around the world, as in such fellow Facebook groups as A Minority within a Minority and many Jewish Facebook groups in Nigeria, Uganda, and Kenya, and in the Western world. Jewish Spirit is inspired by the teachings of such rabbis as Baal Shem Tov, Nachman of Breslov, Abraham Joshua Heschel, Menachem Mendel Schneerson, Zalman Schachter-Shalomi, Adin Steinsaltz, David S. Wolpe, Laura Duhan-Kaplan, Heather Ellen Miller, Shai Specht-Sandler, and Shmuly Yanklowitz, in chronological order. Jewish Spirit members are rabbis, Jewish educators, teachers, scholars, members of various other professions, students, other clergy, and others, in this order. Jewish Spirit pursues parallels in Buddhism, Yoga, Sufism, and other spiritual traditions. The vast majority of us are Jewish, but there are Christians, Moslems, Buddhists, Hindus, and adherents of other faiths, in approximately this order, who stand with their Jewish brothers and sisters, or who simply wish to learn more about us, our beliefs, and our history. Jewish Spirit does not accept advertising or commercial activity; but if you are writing on Jewish subjects or creating Jewish music, arts, or crafts, please share with us. Naturally, do not proselytize or disrespect others. 
                </div>

                 Atheism
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 "Legal and social discrimination against atheists in some places may lead some to deny or conceal their atheism due to fears of persecution. A 2006 study by researchers at the University of Minnesota involving a poll of 2,000 households in the United States found atheists to be the most distrusted of minorities, more so than Muslims, recent immigrants, gays and lesbians, and other groups. Many of the respondents associated atheism with immorality, including criminal behaviour, extreme materialism, and elitism." -Wikipedia, Demographics of Atheism, Discrimination "A 1995 survey attributed to the Encyclopædia Britannica indicates that the non-religious are about 14.7% of the world's population, and atheists around 3.8%. Another survey attributed to Britannica shows the population of atheists at around 2.4% of the world's population." -Wikipedia, Demographics of atheism, Distribution "Furthermore, atheists may not report themselves as such, to prevent suffering from social stigma, discrimination, and persecution in certain regions. Despite these problems, most studies indicate that the non-religious make up about 12-15% of the world's population." -Wikipedia, Demographics of atheism Rules are available here: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1l1oK00e0gXjN1dNpNw99XV_Bg23tqlRcRl-46jZKeyw/edit?usp=sharing Please read before posting!                 </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 《淨土法門疑難問題解答》 李炳南居士原著 雪廬講堂印經功德會編印叢書獻言 「李炳南居士紀念文教基金會」成立的宗旨，在於繼承雪廬老人遺志，發揚老人弘法利生的精神，弘揚儒佛文化，協助政府推行社會教育。因此，我們設置了雪廬紀念講堂，除定期舉辦佛教文化講座外，並在講堂中附設印經功德會，編印通俗性佛教叢書，印贈初入佛門的同修，及社會上不了解佛教的人士，使他們正確的認識佛教，由起信而理解，由理解而實踐，進而解脫煩惱，獲得身心自在。 近年來社會上思想混亂，邪說充斥，五花八門的新教派，像雨後春筍似的冒出來，說通靈，說神通，說靈魂出竅，說世界末日，使好神奇者趨之若騖，也使想以宗教安身立命的人士眼花撩亂，無所適從。 雪廬講堂印經功德會，是以弘揚佛陀正法的理念，來選印經書。凡是涉及外道邪說，附佛法外道謬論，以及荒誕不經的迷信書籍，一概在摒棄之列。我們印經會同仁，是以負責認真的態度，介紹佛陀思想，佛教文化，佛法修持的方法；我們印出的書籍，必可代表佛法聖潔與純正的一面。 雪廬講堂印經功德會草創伊始，根基未固，尚賴我佛們同修、社會各界，予以扶植與支持是幸。 于凌波 八十四年八月於雪廬紀念講堂

              <div class="_8uly">
               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 GREAT HINDUISM
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Fast Facts about Hinduism Religion: Existence Since: Hinduism is the world’s oldest known religion. History of Hinduism can be traced back to 5000-10,000 B.C. Facts about size and Rank: It is the third largest religion of the world with more than 1 billion followers. Location: Most of the Hindus live in India, Nepal, and Sri Lanka with considerable presence in all other parts of the world also. About 85% of Hindus live in India. That is why India is also called as “Hindustan.” Known as: People who follow Hinduism are called as “Hindus.” Hinduism is also known as “Hindu Dharma” (हिंदू धर्म), ” Hindu Religion, “Sanatan Dharma (Eternal Religion),” “Vedic Religion,” or Vedic Dharma. Founder: Hinduism has no single founder. It has been evolving over the thousands of years and will continue to. Origin: Hinduism originated in India. Hinduism is largely based on the teachings from Vedas. Meaning of the word: The word “Hinduism” actually has no real meaning because Hinduism was not founded as a religion. The name “Hindu” is given by the people outside of the India, especially Greeks and Arabs, to those living in the vicinity of “Sindhu” river. So, the way of life those people were following is called “Hinduism.” What do they worship: Hindus believe in one God named as “Brahman” but view other Gods and Goddesses as manifestations of Him. Therefore, in practice, they worship more than one God. Most Hindus worship God in the form of an idol. Rivers, mountains, trees, animals, and natural things which are useful for a human being are revered in Hinduism. Cow is the most revered animal for Hindus. Place of Worship: The place of worship of Hindus is called as a temple. Main Deities: Lord Brahma, Lord Vishnu, and Lord Shiva are the creator, protector, and destroyer respectively. These are the three main deities in Hinduism. Besides them, Lord Ganesha, Lord Krishna, Lord Hanuman, Lord Rama, and Goddess Parvati are the most popular deities in Hinduism. Yugas: According to Hinduism, as there are four seasons in a year, there are four Yugas namely Satya-Yuga, Treta-Yuga, Dvapara-Yuga, Kali-Yuga. At the end of a full cycle of four Yogas, the life on the earth comes to an end (though not completely) and a new era starts. The humanity enters into a new era. The present era is known as Kali-Yuga i.e. Dark Age. Facts about sects in Hinduism: Hinduism consists of different sects like Shaivism, Vaishnavism, and Shaktism. The common people follow all the three sects collectively worshiping Lord Shiva, Lord Vishnu, and Devi. Aims of life: Dharma (righteousness), Artha (wealth), Kama (desire), and Moksha (salvation) are the four objectives of a Hindu’s life. Goal: Salvation is the ultimate goal of a Hindu’s life. Stages of life: According to Hinduism, four stages of life are Brahmcharyashram (Student phase), Grihastahshram (Living with wife and children), Vanprasthashram (leaving the home and pray to God, may keep contact with family), and Sanyasashram (discard everything in life including wife, children, and material things). Contribution: Yoga, Pranayama, meditation, Ayurveda, vegetarianism, and meditation are the best gifts of Hinduism to the world. Tantric sex, Palmistry, acupressure, acupuncture, Jyotish Shastra, martial art, and many other ancient wonders originated in India and are parts of Hinduism Religion. Hinduism is the source of inspiration for three other major religions of the world viz. Buddhism, Sikhism, and Jainism. Zero, point system, and decimal system were invented in India. On the basis of which the modern science exists. Symbols: Aum and Swastika are the main symbols of Hinduism. Besides those, Kalash, Trishul, Tilak, Lingam, Shri, and Yantra are other popular Hindu symbols. The saffron is the official color of Hinduism and the saffron flag is the official flag of Hindus. Sacred Books or Scriptures: Four Vedas, Upanishadas, Bhagvadgita, 18 Puranas, Ramayana, and Mahabharata are the sacred books of Hindus. Language: Most of the Hindu scriptures are written in Sanskrit. Sanskrit is considered to be the mother of all the languages. Sanskrit is considered to be the language of demi-Gods. The languages Hindus use vary according to regions. They speak all the India languages like Hindi, Marathi, Tamil, Telugu, Bengali, Malyalam, Gujarati, Kashmiri, etc. Outside India, the languages spoken by Hindus are English, Sinhali, Indonesian, etc. Eating Habits: Most of the Hindus do not eat beef and/or pork. They also do not eat non-vegetarian food on auspicious days. Hinduism strongly advocates vegetarianism. Food is highly revered and wasting the food is considered as a very bad habit. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 南無大願大孝地藏王菩薩（修學地藏三經）
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                  地藏菩薩（梵語：क्षितिगर्भ Kṣitigarbha），音譯為「乞叉底蘗婆」，常稱幽冥教主。因其「安忍不動如大地，靜慮深密如秘藏」，故名地藏。為漢傳佛教四大菩薩之一，與觀音、文殊、普賢一起，深受世人敬仰。以其「久遠劫來屢發弘願」，即在於『眾生度盡、方證菩提；地獄不空、誓不成佛』故被尊稱為大願地藏菩薩。 《地藏三經》是以闡揚地藏菩薩法門為主的三部經典，分別為唐三藏法師實叉難陀譯的《地藏菩薩本願經》、唐三藏法師玄奘譯的《大乘大集地藏十輪經》、隋外國沙門菩提登譯的《占察善惡業報經》。 夢參老和尚開示：在《地藏經》裡，釋迦牟尼佛跟觀世音菩薩說，修地藏法門的念聖號就好了。一個是讀經，一個是念聖號，這是《地藏經》修行最方便的法門。假使外頭客觀有很多障礙、很多的煩惱，使你沒辦法修行，你念念地藏菩薩該可以吧？一天抽一個小時念一部《地藏經》，不管是否你的心散亂也好，別的什麼都沒有，只要你念《地藏經》、念一千聲地藏聖號，能念一萬聲更好，這是《地藏經》修行法門。 《占察善惡業報經》則說你有業、有業障，因此定慧修習不成。乃至你周邊人事的環境、所有的俗務，你都可以用占察輪來占察，這是特殊方便。修行什麼呢？修行定慧──止觀雙運。二種觀道，一實境界，修觀就是定和慧，然後達到入法界，達到一實境界。 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》告訴你怎樣修，前頭跟你講清楚了，怎麼樣懺悔，怎麼樣起修，就是修定。定依著什麼呢？定就是觀，觀就是思惟修。這個經上跟你講的是靜慮，說你靜下來好好思慮，慮就是觀，靜就是止。 地藏菩薩的專經主要有三種：一者地藏十輪經，二者地藏占察經，三者地藏本願經，即佛弟子口中常說的地藏三經。 地藏十輪經即《大乘大集地藏十輪經》（《大方廣十輪經》應是另一譯本）。 地藏占察經即《占察善惡業報經》，其中有介紹占察木輪法門，我們在修行中或是日常生活中如果遇到痛苦、危難、憂惱等自己無力解決的困難時，可以直接從地藏菩薩那裡得到幫助，這一法門對於末法眾生是非常殊勝的，非常值得修習。 地藏本願經即《地藏菩薩本願經》。地藏菩薩是釋迦佛涅槃之後彌勒佛未來之前的代理佛，在末法時代，地藏法門對娑婆世界的眾生攝受力最大，因緣最深。 明朝蓮池大師專門弘揚淨土，他就提倡地藏三經。後來到蕅益大師，時至明末，專門提倡地藏三經，希望大家能夠重視起來。 《地藏菩薩本願經》 《地藏菩薩本願經》拼音版 忉利天宮神通品第一 《地藏菩薩本願經》 分身集會品第二 《地藏菩薩本願經》觀眾生業緣品第三 《地藏菩薩本願經》閻浮眾生業感品第四 《地藏菩薩本願經》地獄名號品第五 《地藏菩薩本願經》如來贊嘆品第六 《地藏菩薩本願經》利益存亡品第七 《地藏菩薩本願經》閻羅王眾贊嘆品第八 《地藏菩薩本願經》稱佛名號品第九 《地藏菩薩本願經》校量佈施功德緣品第十 《地藏菩薩本願經》地神護法品第十一 《地藏菩薩本願經》見聞利益品第十二 《地藏菩薩本願經》囑累人天品第十三 《地藏菩薩本願經》漫畫版 《地藏菩薩本願經》漫畫版【上】 《地藏菩薩本願經》漫畫版【中】 《地藏菩薩本願經》漫畫版【下】 《占察善惡業報經》 《占察善惡業報經》拼音版卷上 《占察善惡業報經》拼音版卷下 《占察善惡業報經》189種輪相淺释(一） 《占察善惡業報經》189種輪相淺釋（二） 《大乘大集十輪經》 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》序 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第一 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第二 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第三 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第四 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第五 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第六 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第七 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第八 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第九 《大乘大集地藏十輪經》卷第十 本平台以弘揚地藏菩薩大願大孝精神和共修地藏三經為主，以五戒十善為準則： 五戒：不殺生、不偷盜、不邪淫、不妄語、不飲酒。佛教認為，這類不道德的行為應該嚴格禁止，所以稱為五戒。 十善：是在五戒的基礎上建立的，約身、口、意三業分成十種。反之，稱為十惡。 身業有三種：不殺、不盜、不邪淫； 口業有四種：不妄語欺騙、不是非兩舌、不惡口傷人、不說綺語(花言巧語討好別人)； 意業有三種：不貪、不嗔、不愚癡。 諸惡莫作 眾善奉行 自淨其意 是諸佛教 佛經中所說：“若人造重罪，作已深自責，懺悔更不造，能拔根本業”。突出懺悔的重要性，但懂得懺悔還不夠，還需修行的六大綱領：「六度」： 布施、持戒為利他， 忍辱、精進為自利， 禪定、智慧為解脫， 「六度」是「六種行之可以從生死苦惱此岸得度到涅槃安樂彼岸的法門」，為成佛必修之科目。 佛法是根據眾生根性，對治不同時期不同情況各種不同眾生毛病的無上妙法。現代社會的各種誘惑比過去增加了很多，眾生造作殺生、偷盜、邪淫、妄語的機會同樣很多，眾生所犯的貪嗔癡三毒罪業也非常重。每個人在修學佛法時，首先都應該從忏除自己的罪業做起，從讀誦《地藏菩薩本願經》這部基礎經典開始，仗佛菩薩慈力，超拔自己的冤親債主歷代宗親。不將這些因果關系理清解決，我們就不能一身輕松地往生淨土，容易被各種業障牽纏，打失正念，又入輪回，受無邊痛苦，錯失千載難逢的良機，豈不可惜？ 因此，我們建議大家每日按照《禮佛大忏悔文》拜忏，速消業障；每日讀誦《地藏經》（或念南無地藏王菩薩），回向自己的冤親債主歷代宗親，離苦得樂往生淨土。在此基礎上，每日念阿彌陀佛，發出切願，求生西方淨土。 萬丈高樓平地起，《地藏經》是基礎，是起點；西方極樂世界是目標，是終點。在業障深重、欲望強烈的現代社會，眾生只有這樣修學，才能得到切實利益，順利往生淨土。 ▌修行方法 一．吃素戒殺 吃素是斷殺戒殺的開始，從此不再為滿足口腹之欲制造新的冤親債主，避免各種疾病災難蔓延，建立一種全新的健康生活。 二．誦經消業 每天念誦《地藏經》，在佛力的加持下，使讀誦者累生累世的冤親債主歷代宗親得到超拔，業障逐漸消除，身心、家庭、事業等相應得到改善。 三．忏悔解怨 依《禮佛大忏悔文》忏悔，在佛前頂禮108 次，真誠祈請 88 尊佛慈悲加持，忏悔眾罪，回向功德，發願斷惡行善，從心中消除罪障。 四．放生還債 放生就是還債，還累生累世以來無數的殺債。還殺債最快的方法就是放生。人類遭受各種疾病、遭遇各種災難及諸多不順，大多是殺業所致。放生可以培養慈悲心，徹底斷掉殺生習氣。 五．行善積福 每日起心動念為別人著想，起一善念，這是心行一善；每日言談舉止中，說一句有益他人的好話，這是口行一善；每日身體力行中，做一件有益他人、有益社會的事，無論大小，這是身行一善。日積月累，身口意逐漸趨於純善，這就是我們往生西方極樂世界的善根福德因緣資糧。 六．念佛成佛 修行的目的是成佛。在每天的生活中，心想佛、耳聽佛、口念佛，甚至將佛號帶進呼吸中，以此斷妄念，得定慧，早日蒙西方三聖接引成佛。 佛法是救度眾生、接引眾生的慈航寶筏。誦經、拜忏、念佛是前進的航道；吃素、行善是航道的護攔；放生則是加速器。地藏七修行方法，從離三途苦，升至人天福，終達無憂國，環環相扣，層層加持，為有緣人保駕護航，往生西方。 
                </div>

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Bhagavad Gita Study Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hariḥ Om. This study group is dedicated to the study of traditional Advaita Vedānta, based on the teachings of Pūjya Swāmi Dayānanda Saraswati ji of Ārśa Vidyā Gurukulam (not to be mistaken for the founder of Ārya Samāj) Pūjya Swāmiji is a traditional teacher of Vedanta. His depth of understanding and keen insight into the human nature makes him that rare teacher who can communicate the subtle vision of advaita to all audiences. He is able to make one see, with immediacy, the truth of oneself as the whole. Swāmiji handles Śāstra as Śabda Pramāṇam; just as eyes are the pramāṇam for rūpam. The importance of Īśvara and Guru is equally stressed in his teachings. With AIM for Sevā, he is doing what many so-called purist advaitins have failed to do. That is to take care of the neglected masses. Thus Pūjya Swāmiji is a living example of a true vedāntin as exemplified in the Śr̥ti. What we strive for here, in this group, is to study, inquire, share what we have learned, and try to remove what Pūjya Swāmiji refers to as self ignorance. Please let us do that peacefully. Śrī Gurubhyo Namaḥ Om tat sat ___________ About Pūjya Swāmiji: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dU201y28Zh8 Ārśa Vidyā Gurukulam Bookstore (US/Canada): http://books.arshavidya.org/ Bookstore (India): http://www.avrpt.com/all-titles.htm Articles by our Āchāryas: www.avgsatsang.org Additionally,you will find many of His videos on youtube and vimeo as well. Will put together a playlist and share in the future

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Kabbalah Consciousness
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is for the spirituality of Kabbalah. Our perspective is that Kabbalah is not a "religion", it is a technology, and more importantly a consciousness (a way of thinking). The technology is the understanding of the cause and effect relationship of how everything is interconnected and when you begin to KNOW that everything is connected and intended, you can, through personal transformation, and a shift in consciousness change your life, your destiny, and this physical reality. This wisdom is the root of many of the worlds largest religions but we do NOT believe that it is for any specific religion, or groups of people. The wisdom did come from and has a very close connection with the Jewish religion, however our perspective is it should be shared and believe it was given to humanity for ALL PEOPLE. It is for everyone with a desire to learn, and together with it we can change this world. There are many who have tried to keep it hidden and away from the outside world and to keep it exclusive to specific groups, but we are part of the movement to change that. Like with any powerful tool it is up to the user to use it in a proper way. We use this board as an open forum to discuss concepts of Kabbalah, and other modes of spirituality and how they relate to the wisdom of Kabbalah. We welcome open discussion and questions, as this was the method of learning of the great Kabbalist Rabbi Shimon (who authored the Zohar, the main text of Kabbalah) and his students. We want to especially welcome this forum to new students who want to learn more about Kabbalah. Although this board is not sponsored or in any way endorsed or connected to the Kabbalah Centre, many of the people here are students of the Kabbalah Centre. If you are new to Kabbalah and want to learn where to start, just post your question and I'm sure many of the students here will be happy to help. One more note, this board is for sharing spirituality, specifically related to Kabbalah and information about this wisdom but is not intended for spam, politics, selling stuff or other blatant non related topics. Some kabbalah related materials for sale may be allowed on occasion but is not the intention of this group, nor do we make or accept money from this. All posts are reviewed but we do not closely vet the material, nor are we responsible for its accuracy. Everyone is free to post, but only subject related posts will be allowed. Thank you so much for your participation and welcome to our group. Please post a question and introduce yourselves!
                </div>

Anyone blocking or insulting an admin will be removed without notice. "The Great Promise of the Immaculate Heart of Mary: I promise to assist at the hour of death, with the graces necessary for salvation, all those who, on the first Saturday of five consecutive months, shall confess, receive Holy Communion, recite five decades of the Rosary, and keep me company for fifteen minutes, while meditating on the fifteen mysteries of the Rosary, with the intention of making reparation to me."

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to this SGI Study and Encourage Group . The Study of the Buddhism of Nichiren Daishonin essence is to strengthen Soka Gakkai International SGI members, believers and friends, to further Study into the depth in it purity and in a form as clearly as possible for anyone to access and practice Buddhism Equals to Daily Life. Without practicing True Buddhism in daily life and showing actual proof of the Buddhism of Nichiren Daishonin, we cannot called ourselves the true Disciples of Nichiren Daishonin and the three SGI Presidents. Encouragement to anyone further strengthen their Power of Faith and the Power of Practice in their lives, thus, practitioners will be able to fuse their lives with another two powers, the Power of The Buddha and the Power of the Law and only when these four Powers are fused in harmony, attaining Buddhahood in this lifetime was possible. Even when one does not practicing Buddhism, he or she can be read the notes from this Facebook and share their views on a constructive ways to improve this site for the benefits of everyone. And the purpose also serve as a propagation that more people will take up the wonderful Faith in the Buddhism of Nichiren Daishonin and the SGI serve to sustain its purity towards eternity. yours feed back is appreciated for the improvement to benefit everyone. The purpose of this site is to serve its SGI members and readers to create values and harmony for a peaceful world for everyone Posts that does not serve such essences are not encourage and will not be approve, posts of advertisements,destructive photos, words that is not in a constructive manner are also not encourage.Buddhism passages and quotes that does not serve the true intent of the purity and essence are strictly disapproved. Traditional and cultural differences that does not serve to strive and strengthen our Buddhist Faith, Practice and Study are advice not to post and questions and answer regarding to our Buddhist practice is to refer to our mentor, SGI President Daisaku Ikeda guidances and encouragement essays. I sincerely hope that I can serve to my utmost best to make this site that can transform everyone lives to serve our beloved people in society and in our countries to create a world of peace that further serve us and our future generations to come. Thank you, David Tan, 11th June, 2016

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Soka Gakkai International
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Soka Gakkai International (SGI) is a lay Buddhist movement linking more than 12 million people around the world. SGI members integrate their Buddhist practice into their daily lives, following the Lotus Sutra based teachings of Nichiren, a 13th-century Japanese Buddhist priest. Just as the lotus blooms in a muddy pond, all people can manifest the Buddha nature--inner resources of courage, wisdom and compassion that can equip them to overcome life's challenges and lead happy and fulfilling lives. As "engaged Buddhists," SGI members aim to create value in any circumstances and contribute to the well-being of others. Their practice sparks a process of ongoing inner transformation and empowerment known as "human revolution." The promotion of peace, culture and education is central to SGI's activities. Website: http://www.sgi.org/

Men of all faiths, traditions, beliefs, and practices are welcome here! We encourage you to share your experiences, thoughts, questions, answers, and expertise with the group. Feel free to post images, links to your blog posts, resources, book reviews, or anything else you think the guys might enjoy! ♂♂♂ HOW TO JOIN ♂♂♂ 1) Read the 'Group Rules' below 2) Click 'Join Group' underneath the member image bar and answer the questions 3) We'll approve you ASAP Once you've been approved... 4) Write an intro on the group wall saying hi and sharing anything about yourself you'd like the group to know - where you are, your path/tradition, your interests, etc. Δ Δ Δ GROUP RULES Δ Δ Δ 1) Integrity, honor, honesty, and compassion are the ways around here! 2) There is an absolute ZERO TOLERANCE policy on hate speech or bullying. 3) Although this group has several admins, it is meant to be community-run. If you want to see a change, please contact us. We welcome feedback, ideas, suggestions, and help! 4) This group is open to men 18 years and older. Men of ALL orientations are welcome here! 5) You are welcome to post links to your books, shops, sites, pages, etc. as long as you are an active member in the group. For-profit pages need to be posted with a personal review/recommendation. Only admins may pin posts. 6) In order to abide by the laws of the land here on Facebook, admins will monitor the wall for any content that may breach the official Facebook rules about sexually explicit/pornographic content. We follow their rules, not ours in this case. 7) We all love eyecandy. However, please do not post random pics without making an earnest attempt at relating your post to some aspect of spirituality. There are plenty of venues for sexy pics, few for spiritual discussion. We prefer to maintain this page for the latter. 8) If you take the time to post a question or comment, please take the time to follow-up and acknowledge the contributions other guys make to your thread. 9) Vaguebooking is punishable by drawing and quartering... and not the fun kind. 10) This is NOT a hookup or dating page. Sexuality is integral to our spirituality, but this is a safe space where the latter is a focus. Please avoid posting random selfies, dating, or hookup requests. 11) Please limit posts to 3 per day in order to allow others to have their posts above the fold. Problems? Trolls? Bullies? Issues? Please contact an admin directly or mention them (@ followed by their name with no spaces) in the post to get their attention. Admins and Moderators: Alfred Gonzalez John Alfwynn Christopher Lung Johnny Energywork Nik Holton Rudi Huber Christopher Alan Cartier-Wells
