                 Life Before the Holocaust
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the group, "Life Before the Holocaust," by the National Library of Israel. This group aims to share stories – the good and the bad - of the Jewish communities that were built and the lives that were lived by Jewish individuals living in countries and towns across the European continent before the start of the Holocaust. Members are welcome to share their stories about their families, their experiences, and the stories they may have heard or learned about along the way. Our group has several guidelines in place to encourage fruitful and pleasant discussions. Please be sure to read them through in the "About" section of the group before you begin to post. Thank you for being a part of our group and for joining us in learning about and preserving the memory of Jewish life before the Holocaust.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Soto Zen Buddhism
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Soto Zen Buddhism is a school of Buddhism founded by Eihei Dogen and Keizan Jokin in 13th century Japan. Soto Zen practice emphasises continuous practice, making your best effort in each instant without goal or profit seeking, that practice and enlightenment are not two. The core of Soto Zen practice is zazen - shikantaza - just wholehearted sitting - dropping off body and mind - the practice of self-affirming/realising samadhi. This is a focused group for people who are practitioners of Soto Zen, or are interested in Soto Zen. Posts that are not obviously oriented towards Soto Zen Buddhism will probably be removed. If not immediately obvious, please be explicit about your post's link to Soto Zen. When posting, try to be open, topical and polite. This group has people with all different levels of experience, and needs to be a safe environment for a beginner's enquiry, as well as for more in depth discussion. Be kind. We ask that you not advertise in this group (this includes local events, links to your zen group's page, commercial and non-commercial); this is to avoid flooding the timeline and obscuring discussion, and recognises the global nature of the membership. This is not a group for discussions about 'general spirituality', nor is flaming, trolling, flooding, spamming, or any other anti-social web behaviour tolerated. Links to topical blog or web articles are welcome. If you think your post has been removed unfairly, please contact an admin - we will try to be as equitable as possible, but mistakes may happen. Moderators are here to keep order and ensure that everyone has a positive experience. In line with common Facebook courtesy, we ask that you not block Admins. These rules are a result of a group discussion where there was a clear preference for 'tightening things up'. 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 A group for disciples and friends to share stories, information about travels, report of events and festivals, etc. about and by H.H. Lokanath Swami Maharaj. (therefore please try to post only related material or it may be subject to deletion). Born in Aravade, a small village in Maharashtra, India, he went to Mumbai for studying. In the year 1971, His Divine Grace A.C. Bhaktivedanta Swami Prabhupada was touring India with his foreign disciples and had organized a pandal program in Mumbai. Intrigued, maharaj attended the whole Hare Krsna Festival and heard from Srila Prabhupada. Wanting to surrender his life to Lord Krishna, he joined Juhu under the able leadership of Giriraj Swami. As he was coming from a traditional Indian family, there was some initial resistance. However, Maharaj not just made them favorable but transformed his entire village into Krishna consciousness by opening a fantastic ISKCON temple. He has been conducting Padyatra, Vrindavan parikrama and is in charge of World holy name. He travels and preaches from the remotest villages in India to cities and universities in developed countries. ***************************************** Facebook groups of Guru Maharaj ***************************************** H.H. Lokanath Swami Maharaj Disciples &amp; Friends [OFFICIAL] group: https://www.facebook.com/groups/H.H.LokanathMaharaj.officialfacebkgroup/ Lovers of bhajans &amp; kirtans by His Holiness Lokanath Swami Maharaja: https://www.facebook.com/groups/128382507536/ Vraja Mandala Darshan Book: https://www.facebook.com/groups/125618287787598/ HH Lokanath Swami Vyasa Puja Offerings: https://www.facebook.com/groups/311807928946832/ Facebook fan page: https://www.facebook.com/LokanathSwami Websites: http://www.lokanathswami.com/ http://www.lokmediaonline.com/ http://www.lokanathswamiblog.com/ http://www.iskconaravade.com/ http://www.iskconnoida.com/ http://www.iskconpandharpur.com/ http://www.lokmediaonline.com http://www.lokanathswamiblog.com http://www.iskconaravade.com http://www.iskconnoida.com http://www.iskconpandharpur.com

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Students and Followers of Geshe Kelsang Gyatso
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was created for the students and followers of Venerable Geshe Kelsang Gyatso Rinpoche and the New Kadampa Tradition (NKT-IKBU). Thank you for joining us! The express purpose of this group is to discuss the meaning of Venerable Geshe-la’s teachings of Kadampa Buddhism, and how we can practice and apply them to our daily lives. This group is an informal, unofficial group established by Geshe-la’s students, and the opinions expressed in the group should in no way be considered to be officially those of the NKT. We welcome discussions on how everyone is practicing and applying Kadam Dharma to daily life! No politics please on this page, only Dharma. We suggest that, before posting anything, we can ask ourselves: is it true, is it kind, and is it helpful? We would also like to encourage everyone that if there are ever any differences of opinion, let's all remember the golden rule "Living beings have no faults." Ad hominem remarks and personal insults will immediately be removed by the moderators. If you are concerned about something appearing to be political, please write to us privately and we will try to solve the problem. We want everyone to feel comfortable here. No matter one’s gender, background, age, race, religion, politics, sexual orientation, or otherwise, everyone is always welcome at all Kadampa Centers and to join in these informal discussions. We believe that everyone can benefit from meditation and Buddha’s teachings. With inner peace, wisdom, and compassion we can all make a better world now and for generations to come. We respect all Buddhist traditions and teachers (both past and present), and we are delighted that Buddhadharma is flourishing on Facebook, but we very much want to keep this page just for discussions relating directly to Geshe Kelsang Gyatso and his presentation of Dharma. This is so that when people come to this page, they are not confused by what they find -- in the same way that if they went to one of his teachings, they would hear him expounding his own special presentation and not that of other teachers or traditions. The group does not authenticate or endorse any articles that are linked to from this group. If the moderators feel that a post or comment is straying too far from the core principles of the page as outlined above, we will ask the person to remove it themselves, pointing out our reasons. If necessary, the moderators will delete posts directly; but when they do so they will send a private message explaining the reasons for doing so. With all best wishes and love, The Moderators
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ALL MEMBERS- READ THIS. Goal — A discussion group of atheists and reasonable, questioning theists deliberating The Thinking Atheist podcast and topics of concern to all. The Golden Rule of Communication: Treat others with the respect you desire. We expect mature conversation. No topics are off limits but we draw the line at immature, racist or hateful posts and comments. Poaching is rude. Ask an admin before suggesting another atheist group. Remain engaged with your OP (Original Post). ‘Like’ comments. Reply to questions. Hone your point. Don’t be a post ghost. Search the hashtag #TTAFQuestion before you post a question-- many have already been asked and are marked with this symbol. Rules: 1) Don't block an admin. You will be removed. If you are, unblock and reapply. 2) Don't be a pain in the neck (troll) or permanent removal is possible. 3) Don't post ads.This includes charity and self-promotion. You will be removed and blocked. 4) No doxxing (posting of private information that is not your own). You will be removed and blocked. If you are doxxed in the group, contact the admins. 5) Do not mention any variation of the phrase "what does this have to do with atheism?" because dammit this is a group FOR atheists, not ABOUT atheism. Violators may be forced to recite the atheist ten commandments, or do a handstand. Listen to the podcast here: http://www.blogtalkradio.com/thethinkingatheist Or on YouTube: http://www.youtube.com/user/TheThinkingAtheist Official Website: http://thethinkingatheist.com/ Official Facebook: https://www.facebook.com/thethinkingatheist/ Common practices of valued group members: • Posts responsibly. Labels their intent in the headline. Responds to comments. • Gets involved. Likes/comments on other posts. • Doesn't get easily shocked or insulted. • Similarly, isn't a gross reporter. Speaks with the author, the group, or the admin first. • Edits before entering. Spelling and grammar sure, but mostly to consider the impact of their words. They ask the question 'Would I want this comment directed towards me?' • Avoids anger in conversation. Take time to formulate the perfect response. We can be our best selves here, given thought. • References stated facts with respected sources, NOT rando Youtube submissions. • Shows tolerance of all ideas and behaviors. • Behaves as the bigger person in conflicts. • Isn't stubborn. • Has a sense of humor! Can't stress that enough. • Most of all -- has fun!

We are related to the Buckland clan .On the left hand margin you will find out what hereditary Witches are and what Romany gypsies Witches are and how the two go together. A clan can be just one family or an unlimited number living together. It is still illegal to be a Witch &amp; read the Tarot, in Jersey. The UK witchcraft laws of 1951 were never repealed in the Channel Islands, so life can be challenging. I am also the High Priestess of "The Coven of the Silver Wheel” I am a 3rd degree Wytch, so I teach others in my Coven and also through workshops. I have also appeared on 103 Peter Macs breakfast show and with Richard Letto at Radio Jersey, Radio 5 Live, ITV Channel news and the Jersey Evening Post as well as Chat its Fate Magazine and 247 magazine. I am also feature on the BBC radio Jersey web site in a discussion about being a Witch and also on the places that inspire my page, I have also held a platform show at Maison Gorey Hotel and taken part in the Hippy Fairs and Psychic Fairs. I have 2 sons who are taught my way of life just as I was. We live a very traditional Romany life we grow and harvest herbs, make our own magical tools and live in accordance with the Old Ways &amp; the Wheel of the Year. I embrace my heritage as do my clan, I read the Tarot every day and have clients from all over the world and many testimonials. There are many pages on this site one of them is called Clan Names if you know you Romany Clan name please add it to the list. Also if you have a Hereditary Wytch linage there is also a page for this again please add you information. I have worked hard to make this site a friendly safe place for people who are like minded and wish to learn any questions please ask. All I ask is that we are all considerate of each other’s thoughts &amp; feelings, and sensitive to all our needs. We are all here to learn and help each other, this is not just a site it is a clan {Irish for family} I hope all who enter here are happy and find a wealth of knowledge, I have no certificates on my walls only a verbal knowledge passed down through the generations and a love of what I do, so come in and join the clan. This site is all my own work and is copyright and not available to be used anywhere else @rhiannagalvinhughes1990. © March of 1990

                 Adamantly Anti-Theist
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Okay. Anti-Theism (Antitheism?) is not a relaxed stance regarding religion. Being an anti-theist means that you realize that religion is positively harmful to humanity, period. It is bad for all of us, and must be attacked. All religion is bad for us. All religion must be attacked constantly, persistently, but peacefully. Religion has used, and still uses, violence consistently to push it's particular brand of insanity upon the rest of us. Some religions are worse than others in this regard, but all are bad for the mind of the individual, and for the collective minds of the memberships of the various cults (all religions are cults). We must attack them relentlessly with facts, logic, reason, science, reality, morality based upon our common humanity rather than bullshit proscriptions invented in the minds of primitive goat herders in the deserts of the middle-east, or of other groups of humans around the Earth. And to sum up, here's an apropos quote from E. Haldeman-Julius....... "“We advocate the atheistic philosophy because it is the only clear, consistent position which seems possible to us. As atheists, we simply deny the assumptions of theism; we declare that the God idea, in all its features, is unreasonable and unprovable; we add, more vitally, that the God idea is an interference with the interests of human happiness and progress. We oppose religion not merely as a set of theological ideas; but we must also oppose religion as a political, social and moral influence detrimental to the welfare of humanity.” ― E. Haldeman-Julius, The meaning of atheism

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 SRI SRI RADHA KRISHNA...Spread the Word...Spread the Love
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 SRI SRI RADHA KRISHNA - SPREAD THE WORD - SPREAD THE LOVE. http://www.stephen-knapp.com/sri_krishna.html LORD SRI KRISHNA IS THE SUPREME ABSOLUTE TRUTH. Absolute Truth refers to a reality which doesn't change over time. Absolute means all other truths are relative to it, or dependant on it. When we talk about God, or Sri Krishna, we're talking about the Absolute Truth. The Absolute Truth is the source of everything, the ultimate cause of all causes. In Sanskrit, it is also called satyam param, the highest truth. This supreme truth can be perceived in three features—as Brahman, all-pervading, impersonal oneness, as Paramatma, the manifestation of God within the heart of every being, and as Bhagavan, the Supreme Personality of Godhead. These three are the same one truth, understood from increasingly advanced levels of realization. In the beginning the Absolute appears impersonal. With more advancement, the Supreme is perceived within one's own heart and the hearts of others. The highest realization is to see the Supreme Truth as the Supreme Person, who is complete in wealth, power, fame, beauty, knowledge, and renunciation. The Bhagavad-gita, the Srimad-Bhagavatam, and other Vedic literatures identify this Supreme Personality of Godhead as Krishna. Brahman exists as the all-pervading energy in this phenomenal world. Therefore the Vedas have defined Brahman as formless, impersonal, pure, and so on. But the source of Brahman is an eternal personality who has no material form but who has a transcendental form full of spiritual potencies and all divine qualities. He is the Supreme Personality of Godhead, the embodiment of eternity, knowledge, and bliss. He possesses all six transcendental opulences to an infinite degree, He performs superexcellent divine pastimes, and He alone is to be searched out and known in all the scriptures. The materialistic, fruitive workers make the mistake of thinking that this supreme transcendental personality is mundane, and thus they become degraded into pseudo-devotees. And the dry speculators, having been repulsed by the material phenomena in their search for knowledge of the Absolute think that the transcendental form of the Supreme Personality of Godhead is also repulsive, thus clearly proving that the ascending process of acquiring knowledge is insufficient and inferior. Both these groups are in a pathetic spiritual state. Therefore, to shower His causeless mercy upon them, the Supreme Lord has revealed the truth about Himself and His transcendental potencies in the Bhagavad-gita.
                </div>
               </div>

                 Zen Philosophy
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome To All New Members! Just One Rule: ***Stay On Topic*** [Please "like" The Zen Philosophy Page at: https://www.facebook.com/alt.philosophy.zen/] Note: When posting to be sure to indicate in what way it is relevant to the subject of Zen Philosophy if it is not obvious, and please always add some comment to any graphic posting if it does not speak for itself. Thank you. Members may discuss the philosophical aspects of Zen, Zen Buddhism or Buddhism beyond tradition or practice and as it relates to similar schools of philosophical thought and related subjects in general. Certainly, discussions can be wide-ranging, but if it is unrelated to the original topic (or the general subject of the Group itself) then it may be removed, in order to keep the thread (and Group) on track. This also applies to queries or comments about moderation, which should not be posted as comments. If you have questions or comments regarding moderation etc, please contact administration directly on the main Zen Philosophy Page: https://www.facebook.com/alt.philosophy.zen/ Please Feel Free to invite all those who you feel may benefit and contribute productively to discussions related to this subject. Let's see if the discussion can bring about new insights and understanding Thanks to All (- -) "A philosopher asked Buddha: 'Without words, without silence, will you tell me the truth?' The Buddha sat quietly. The philosopher then bowed and thanked the Buddha, saying, 'With your loving kindness I have cleared away my delusions and entered the true path.' After the philosopher had gone, Ananda asked Buddha what the philosopher had attained. The Buddha commented, 'A good horse runs even at the shadow of the whip.'" Note: It seems an explanation for the second entry question "Do you realize that to think Zen Philosophy is a contradiction in terms is to have a Zen Philosophy?" might be in order. The question is an attempt to pre-empt objections made in the past about how Zen and Philosophy are contrary as Zen is often posited to not be about ratiocination. The question points out that even to express such an objection is to contradict the statement of objection itself since to say that Zen is not about ratiocination (or Philosophy) is a Zen Philosophy or a Philosophical idea about Zen. Add to this that the objection is definitively and precisely Off Topic and the one rule is to Stay On Topic. Furthermore, It raises the question of why anyone who thinks that Zen and Philosophy are contrary would join the group, to begin with. Hopefully, this clarifies things. May all living entities become calm by practicing bhakti-yoga, for by accepting devotional service they will think of each other's welfare.               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 A Daily Dose of Talmud: Daf Yomi for Everyone
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to My Jewish Learning’s daily Talmud study group! This is your space to ask questions, share observations, and discuss one of Judaism’s most sacred and beloved texts: the Talmud. Around the world, tens of thousands of Jews participate in Daf Yomi (literally “a page a day”) — a program to read through the entire Talmud, one page every day. Since the Talmud is 2,711 pages, that takes about seven and a half years. January 5, 2020 marks the beginning of the next cycle — the 14th since the “world’s largest book club” began on Rosh Hashanah in 1923. My Jewish Learning offers a daily email for the first tractate of the Talmud, tractate Berakhot, which deals with Jewish blessings. Berakhot will be read from January 5 to March 6, 2020. You can sign up here to receive a daily email about each page in your inbox: https://www.myjewishlearning.com/get-your-daily-dose-of-talmud/ We call this series “A Daily Dose of Talmud: Daf Yomi for Everyone” because it is meant to be accessible to both newbies and people who have studied Talmud for a long time but know, like the ancient rabbinic sage Ben Bag Bag, that if you keep turning it and turning it, you will find more, indeed everything, in its pages. IF you're joining us later in the cycle, or would like to go back and read previous emails, or even get a bit ahead, you can always view everything that has been published in our archive, updated daily. We publish the emails online 18 hours before we actually send them: https://www.myjewishlearning.com/category/study/jewish-texts/berakhot/ We encourage you to sign up for our email series, and then come discuss what you’re learning on this page. Talmud is traditionally learned with a havruta — a peer partner. In this group, thanks to the wonders of technology, you'll have many! Even if you don’t follow along with our emails, you are welcome here to discuss Talmud — especially the page of the day — as long as you are respectful and curious. Welcome! 
                </div>
               </div>

                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">8,405 位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">14 篇新帖</span></span>
                </div>

Please prayerfully consider your membership here if you are in disagreement with our Distinctives. If you choose to stay, even though you disagree with our beliefs, then we ask that you be an example of a mature Christian and not practice posting controversial subjects, "baiting" arguments, or drive-by rants against us before leaving, or being removed. Of course we welcome any questions or comments, but simply ask that you do so privately to one of our admins. We will do the best that we can to answer. The Calvary Distinctives... (9 of the 11) ◦Calvary Chapel seeks to declare the whole counsel of God (Acts 20:27), believing that the best program to achieve this is a systematic study of the entire Bible in an expositional manner. ◦Calvary Chapel looks to the New Testament book of Acts as the divine model for the Church. ◦Calvary Chapel recognizes the experience of the empowering work of the Holy Spirit as distinct and usually separate from the indwelling of the Spirit that occurs at the point of salvation. ◦Calvary Chapel practices a relaxed, casual style of ministry. We do not allow spiritual hype to motivate people, but rely on the teaching of God's Word coupled with the ministry of the Holy Spirit. ◦Calvary Chapel places a large emphasis on God's grace recognizing that we are saved by grace and stand in grace. ◦Calvary Chapel emphasizes the centrality of Jesus Christ in all things. He is the reason we meet and the One whom we serve. We seek to eliminate anything that places undo focus on anyone or anything but Christ. ◦Calvary Chapel is solidly pre-tribulation and pre-millennial in our eschatology. ◦Calvary Chapel believes in a balance between the biblical concepts of God's Sovereign election and man's responsibility. ◦Calvary Chapel believes in the supremacy of love - without which all the gifts of the Spirit are useless. The main purpose of the page is to fellowship, encourage, pray, share excitement about prophecy, and from time to time, point out errors within the Church (which is rare here if we indeed follow the distinctives. Any posts that go against the distinctives, are overtly argumentative, or have some new theology that can’t be supported by at least 2 solid biblical references, will be removed at our discretion... Prohibited: arguing/bickering, swearing, threatening, donations/GoFundMe, or post nudity/pornography or spam will be removed &amp; timeouts implemented: 1st offense: 24 hour time out (1 day) 2nd offense: 72 hour time out (3 days) 3rd offense: 1 week time out (7 days) 4th offense: permanent removal/ban from group. In Christ Jesus, our Glorious God and Savior, CCN Admins

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 ♥ LIGHTWORKERS of THE WORLD ♥
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 LIGHTWORKERS POSTING GUIDELINES The purpose of Lightworkers of the World is to accelerate the evolution of humanity by raising vibration of self and others. We are a group where members can read educational and uplifting material, participate in discussions, and give/receive support, love, advice and healing. We reserve the right to delete any posts that we feel are inappropriate for this group. PLAY NICE: We will not tolerate abusive or harassing comments. If you cannot present your ideas politely you may be removed from the group. Name-calling is NOT acceptable. LIVE FEEDS: Members may NOT post active live feeds in this group. PERSONAL POSTS: Lightworkers of the World is a community. You are welcome to post questions, ask for healing, support or advice, or simply introduce yourself to the group. Please note that posting of another person’s picture requires their permission. SELFIES: We believe that providing positive feedback can help boost the spirit of those who are struggling or seeking motivation. We also believe the best growth comes when the poster interacts with those giving feedback. Posts with a picture that only says ‘What do you see’ will be deleted’. If you truly want feedback, tell us a bit about yourself, your desires and your challenges first. From there we will be happy to respond. ADVERTISING: We are not here to be a target market. If a post asks for money or donations it will be deleted. We do not allow advertising of products or services. We will allow promotion of groups and pages related to Lightwork along with sharing of educational material. We anticipate that members who promote are also active participants in the community. SOLICITATION: We do not allow solicitation of clients. We will delete posts that offer healing or readings that require members to send private messages to proceed. PICKING POSTS: Posts that encourage people to ‘pick for a reading’, such as pick a tarot card, pick a crystal, etc. are limited to MONDAY ONLY. On Tuesday we will turn off comments for these posts so they gracefully fade away. OBVIOUS DELETIONS: Pornography, graphic violence, animal abuse and messages invoking hatred or anger do not belong on this page. POLITICAL POSTS: We will delete any posts that state a position either for or against a political candidate. We are non-political and take a neutral position. RELIGIOUS POSTS: Lightwork transcends. We do not accept posts that sell a religious viewpoint or imply others are deficient for following a different path. TIMEWASTERS: We will delete posts that provide no value while attracting comments, such as math puzzles, games, or posts that ask for ‘Yes’ or ‘Amen’ or other repetitive answers. CLICKBAIT POSTS: Even if the information is valid, we are not here to train people about health issues, proper diet, exercise routines or celebrity news. EVALUATION OF VALIDITY: We cannot attest to the value of any services of any members. Let the buyer beware.

𝘌𝘷𝘦𝘳𝘺𝘵𝘩𝘪𝘯𝘨 𝘧𝘳𝘰𝘮 𝘌𝘱𝘪𝘴𝘵𝘦𝘮𝘰𝘭𝘰𝘨𝘺, 𝘔𝘦𝘵𝘢𝘱𝘩𝘺𝘴𝘪𝘤𝘴, 𝘗𝘩𝘪𝘭𝘰𝘴𝘰𝘱𝘩𝘺 𝘰𝘧 𝘔𝘪𝘯𝘥, 𝘢𝘯𝘥 𝘖𝘯𝘵𝘰𝘭𝘰𝘨𝘺, 𝘵𝘰 𝘊𝘰𝘴𝘮𝘰𝘭𝘰𝘨𝘺 𝘢𝘯𝘥 𝘗𝘩𝘪𝘭𝘰𝘴𝘰𝘱𝘩𝘺 𝘰𝘧 𝘚𝘤𝘪𝘦𝘯𝘤𝘦 𝘢𝘳𝘦 𝘧𝘢𝘪𝘳 𝘨𝘢𝘮𝘦 𝘧𝘰𝘳 𝘥𝘪𝘴𝘤𝘶𝘴𝘴𝘪𝘰𝘯 𝘢𝘴 𝘭𝘰𝘯𝘨 𝘢𝘴 𝘪𝘵’𝘴 𝘵𝘪𝘦𝘥 𝘪𝘯, 𝘤𝘰𝘯𝘯𝘦𝘤𝘵𝘦𝘥, 𝘰𝘳 𝘤𝘰𝘯𝘵𝘳𝘢𝘴𝘵𝘦𝘥 𝘸𝘪𝘵𝘩 𝘉𝘶𝘥𝘥𝘩𝘪𝘴𝘵 𝘗𝘩𝘪𝘭𝘰𝘴𝘰𝘱𝘩𝘺. Neither Christianity nor Islam is based on the birthdate of Jesus Christ, or on Santa Claus, Valentine's, April Fool's Day, or Easter bunnies ☆ All threats of violence, including masked/veiled threats, will result in the offender being banned and immediately reported to the proper authorities ☆ No heretical teachings Thank you for your cooperation.               <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Four Horsemen of the Anti-Apocalypse: Dawkins, Dennett, Harris and Hitchens
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group is to salute, discuss, promote and advance the thinking of the four leaders of the new zeitgeist in rationalism (not atheism any more, in respect of Mr. Harris): Richard Dawkins, Daniel Dennett, Sam Harris and Christopher Hitchens. *The God Delusion: Dawkins *Breaking the Spell: Dennett *The end of Faith: Harris *god is not Great: Hitchens ------------------------------------------------------------------- An open letter to Messrs. Dawkins, Dennett, Harris and Hitchens By Michael Shermer Since the turn of the millennium, a new militancy has arisen among religious skeptics in response to three threats to science and freedom: (1) attacks against evolution education and stem cell research; (2) breaks in the barrier separating church and state leading to political preferences for some faiths over others; and (3) fundamentalist terrorism here and abroad. Among many metrics available to track this skeptical movement is the ascension of four books to the august heights of the New York Times best-seller list — Sam Harris’s Letter to a Christian Nation (Knopf, 2006), Daniel Dennett’s Breaking the Spell (Viking, 2006), Christopher Hitchens’s God Is Not Great (Hachette Book Group, 2007) and Richard Dawkins’s The God Delusion (Houghton Mifflin, 2006) — that together, in Dawkins’s always poignant prose, “raise consciousness to the fact that to be an atheist is a realistic aspiration, and a brave and splendid one. You can be an atheist who is happy, balanced, moral and intellectually fulfilled.” Amen, brother. Whenever religious beliefs conflict with scientific facts or violate principles of political liberty, we must respond with appropriate aplomb. Nevertheless, we should be cautious about irrational exuberance. I suggest that we raise our consciousness one tier higher for the following reasons. 1. Anti-something movements by themselves will fail. Atheists cannot simply define themselves by what they do not believe. As Austrian economist Ludwig von Mises warned his anti-Communist colleagues in the 1950s: “An anti-something movement displays a purely negative attitude. It has no chance whatever to succeed. Its passionate diatribes virtually advertise the program they attack. People must fight for something that they want to achieve, not simply reject an evil, however bad it may be.” 2. Positive assertions are necessary… 3. Rational is as rational does. If it is our goal to raise people’s consciousness to the wonders of science and the power of reason, then we must apply science and reason to our own actions. It is irrational to take a hostile or condescending attitude toward religion because by doing so we virtually guarantee that religious people will respond in kind… 4. The golden rule is symmetrical. In the words of the greatest conscious­ness raiser of the 20th century, Mart­in Luther King, Jr., in his epic “I Have a Dream” speech: “In the process of gaining our rightful place, we must not be guilty of wrong­ful deeds. Let us not seek to satisfy our thirst for freedom by drinking from the cup of bitterness and hatred. We must forever conduct our struggle on the high plane of dignity and discipline.” If atheists do not want theists to prejudge them in a negative light, then they must not do unto theists the same. 5. Promote freedom of belief and disbelief. A higher moral principle that encompasses both science and religion is the freedom to think, believe and act as we choose, so long as our thoughts, beliefs and actions do not infringe on the equal freedom of others. As long as religion does not threaten science and freedom, we should be respectful and tolerant because our freedom to disbelieve is inextricably bound to the freedom of others to believe. As King, in addition, noted: “The marvelous new militancy which has engulfed the Negro community must not lead us to a distrust of all white people, for many of our white brothers, as evidenced by their presence here today, have come to realize that their destiny is tied up with our destiny. And they have come to realize that their freedom is inextricably bound to our freedom.” Rational atheism values the truths of science and the power of reason, but the principle of freedom stands above both science and religion. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Our Sephardic Family
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Background Our Sephardic Family is a Facebook group created in 2011 by Mark Angel. It has grown to 4000+ members on 6 continents. This group is comprised mainly of Sephardic members, but others have joined because of their interest Sephardiem are descendants of Jews fled from the Iberian Peninsula (what is now Spain and Portugal). Vision The vision of this group is to share our heritage and to better understand our mutual Sephardic history. Our goal is to connect Sephardics, and strengthen the concept of family and common cultural bonds. We hope to share knowledge of our precious customs, foods, dress, language and rituals so we leave empowered and inspired through our culture. This will contribute toward our future legacy and help preserve precious Sephardic heritage. Interesting demographics about Our Sephardic Family: Total number of countries: 67 ---- Top 10 countries represented: United States,Israel,Turkey,South Africa,Mexico,United Kingdom,Canada,Brazil,Belgium,France ---- Gender: Male~40% ; Female~60%

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Buddha Quotes
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Gautama Buddha, most commonly known as Buddha, was an ascetic and sage and the founder of the teaching of Buddhism. Historians believe he was born Prince Siddhartha Gautama in the 5th or 6th Century BC in Nepal. In his 20s, the prince experienced realities of the outside world that led him on a quest for enlightenment. He left the palace to search for it and eventually attained enlightenment. It was then that he became Buddha. Until he died at the age of 80, Buddha taught many people how to achieve enlightenment. His doctrines eventually became what are known as Buddhism. Buddhism has been a guiding light for spiritual seekers for over 2500 years. Buddhism is a very calm, peaceful and fair way of life and these Buddha quotes encompass the philosophy of Buddha’s teachings. He's known by many names to many people but to me he's just Buddha. Find and save ideas about Buddha quote “Doubt everything. Find your own light.” – Buddha You will not be punished for your anger; you will be punished by your anger. Do not dwell in the past, do not dream of the future, concentrate the mind on the present moment. Holding on to anger is like grasping a hot coal with the intent of throwing it at someone else; you are the one who gets burned. Webpage : http://inspiring-quotes2.blogspot.com

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 MUSLIM MOMMIES OF CALIFORNIA
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Muslim Mommies of California. As a Muslim mommy myself, I realized we are lacking a forum where we can discuss relevant topics as moms, professionals, wives, daughters, friends, business owners and most of all sisters! Let's join together and create a crowd sourced page where we can discuss mommy advice, set up play dates, share our mommy businesses, recipes, share halal restaurant hot spots and an overall support group for fellow muslim mommies. Let's work together to strengthen our community relationships in an effort to raise a Strong Muslim Youth who will be positive and successful contributors to society &amp; Islam. Feel free to share ideas, topics, questions but remember to follow the rules below: * First and foremost, we will all remain respectful towards one another. There will be a zero tolerance policy for bashing, derogatory comments and profanity. If you wouldn't want your child to see it or repeat it please don't post it. * No political posts please. * If you would like opinions on a sensitive topic you can private message the admin your question, I will then post it anonymously to the forum so you can gather some opinions without exposing your identity. Please keep in mind I may get inundated with requests so feel free to follow up message me if you don't see your post within 10 days. * When giving and receiving medical opinions please keep in mind they are exactly that, only opinions and you should consult physicians for all applied medical advice. Fellow mommies can only offer their personal experience which may or may not be applicable. To search the group click on the magnifying glass on the top right and search for the word in the post. Reporting posts. Please report posts that don't follow these rules to the admin by clicking top right of the post. This will only notify the admin who will then evaluate and remedy the post. Advertisement Rules: Please limit your posts promoting your business to the FIRST day of the month on a post designated for advertising. By becoming a member of Muslim Mommies of California you agree that you will evaluate, and bear all risks associated with the use of any content and that under no circumstances will Muslim Mommies of California be liable in any way for any content, private messages, posts or for any loss or damage of any kind incurred as a result of the use of any content posted, emailed or otherwise made available via the group. You acknowledge that LA Mommies does not pre-screen or approve content, but that it shall have the right (but not the obligation) in its sole discretion to refuse, delete or move any content.
